CBS LOAN VARIATION AND WAIVER DEED

Version 7 — Corrected & Aligned

CBS GROUP PTY LTD

and

WATER ROADS PTY LTD

DATE: [INSERT EXECUTION DATE]

CONFIDENTIAL

Changes from V6: Recap Deed date corrected (14→15 Jan). Share numbers corrected in Recital D (pre-split 100K, post-split 1M). Execution date changed to placeholder. CBS Consent cross-ref dates removed. CBS execution block requires two signatories. Conflict disclosure added. Loan Agreement date flagged (31 Aug vs 1 Aug).

PARTIES

1.	CBS GROUP PTY LTD ACN 164 870 080 of [INSERT CBS ADDRESS — verify against ASIC extract] (Lender or CBS)

2.	WATER ROADS PTY LTD ACN 686 900 014 of Unit 142, 19 Hickson Road, Dawes Point NSW 2000 (Borrower or Company)

RECITALS

A.	The Lender and the Borrower are parties to a secured loan agreement dated [INSERT LOAN DATE — verify: 1 August or 31 August 2025] (as amended, varied, or supplemented from time to time) (the Loan Agreement) pursuant to which the Lender has provided a loan facility to the Borrower.

B.	The Loan Agreement contains certain covenants, undertakings, and events of default, including provisions relating to:

(i)	change of control of the Borrower;

(ii)	negative pledge restrictions;

(iii)	ownership restructuring; and

(iv)	other matters that may be triggered by the Recapitalisation (as defined below).

C.	The Borrower, together with its shareholders CobaltBlu Pty Ltd and CBS, has implemented a recapitalisation of the Borrower (the Recapitalisation) pursuant to a Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026 (the Recapitalisation Deed).

D.	The Recapitalisation involved:

(i)	the cancellation of all existing shares in the Borrower (being 1,000 FOU/Founder’s shares held by CobaltBlu and 100 Class B shares held by CBS);

(ii)	the issue of 100,000 new shares (96,000 F Shares to CobaltBlu and 4,000 Common Shares to CBS);

(iii)	a 10-for-1 share split, increasing total share count to 1,000,000 shares (960,000 F Shares and 40,000 Common Shares); and

(iv)	the adoption of an amended and restated constitution (V3.1, effective 15 January 2026).

E.	The Borrower anticipates completing a Series A equity financing (the Series A) following the Recapitalisation, which will involve the issue of preferred shares to new investors and may result in changes to the ownership structure of the Borrower.

F.	The Lender wishes to:

(i)	waive certain provisions of the Loan Agreement that would otherwise be triggered by the Recapitalisation and/or the Series A;

(ii)	vary certain provisions of the Loan Agreement to permit the Recapitalisation and the Series A;

(iii)	subordinate the Loan Agreement to the Series A financing; and

(iv)	commit to full discharge of the Loan Agreement at Series A completion.

G.	Jeffrey Alan Dusting is a director of both the Borrower and the Lender. He is also a director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd and the spouse of Sarah Margaret Taylor (director and Company Secretary of the Borrower, and director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu). The parties have managed these conflicts through standing notices under section 192 of the Corporations Act, verbal disclosures at the board meetings of 15 January 2026 (WaterRoads) and 16 January 2026 (CBS), and Jeffrey Alan Dusting’s abstention from all CBS votes on the Recapitalisation. Jim Ellwood, as independent CBS director, has been authorised to execute all CBS-side documents.

OPERATIVE PROVISIONS

1.	DEFINITIONS AND INTERPRETATION

1.1	Definitions

In this Deed, unless the context otherwise requires:

“Board” means the board of directors of the Borrower from time to time.

“Business Day” means a day that is not a Saturday, Sunday or public holiday in Sydney, New South Wales.

“Corporations Act” means the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth).

“Effective Date” means 15 January 2026, being the date on which the Recapitalisation became effective in accordance with the Recapitalisation Deed.

“Event of Default” has the meaning given in the Loan Agreement.

“Loan Agreement” means the secured loan agreement dated [INSERT LOAN DATE] between the Lender and the Borrower (as amended, varied, or supplemented from time to time, including by this Deed).

“Negative Pledge” means any negative pledge covenant in the Loan Agreement.

“Permitted Security Interest” has the meaning given in clause 3.2.

“Recapitalisation” has the meaning given in Recital C.

“Recapitalisation Deed” has the meaning given in Recital C.

“Review Event” has the meaning given in the Loan Agreement (if applicable).

“Security” means any security interest granted by the Borrower in favour of the Lender under or in connection with the Loan Agreement.

“Series A” has the meaning given in Recital E.

“Series A Investor” means any investor that subscribes for shares in the Borrower as part of the Series A, and includes any security trustee or nominee acting on behalf of such investors.

1.2	Interpretation

In this Deed, unless the context otherwise requires:

(a)	headings are for convenience only and do not affect interpretation;

(b)	the singular includes the plural and vice versa;

(c)	a reference to a party includes that party’s successors and permitted assigns;

(d)	a reference to a clause or Annexure is a reference to a clause of, or Annexure to, this Deed;

(e)	a reference to the Loan Agreement includes any amendment, variation, or supplement to the Loan Agreement, including this Deed;

(f)	where a word or phrase is defined, other grammatical forms of that word or phrase have corresponding meanings; and

(g)	a reference to “$” or “dollars” is a reference to Australian dollars.

2.	WAIVERS — RECAPITALISATION

2.1	Change of Control Waiver

The Lender irrevocably waives any right to:

(a)	treat the Recapitalisation as a “change of control”, “change of ownership”, “ownership restructuring”, or similar event under the Loan Agreement;

(b)	declare an Event of Default, Review Event, or similar event under the Loan Agreement as a result of the Recapitalisation;

(c)	accelerate, demand early repayment of, or otherwise enforce the Loan Agreement as a result of the Recapitalisation;

(d)	exercise any other right or remedy under the Loan Agreement that would otherwise be triggered by the Recapitalisation; or

(e)	claim that the Recapitalisation constitutes a breach of any covenant, undertaking, or obligation under the Loan Agreement.

2.2	Ownership Percentage Waiver

The Lender acknowledges and agrees that:

(a)	the reduction in CBS’s percentage shareholding in the Borrower from 9.09% to 4.00% as a result of the Recapitalisation does not trigger any rights or remedies under the Loan Agreement;

(b)	the increase in CobaltBlu’s percentage shareholding in the Borrower from 90.91% to 96.00% as a result of the Recapitalisation does not trigger any rights or remedies under the Loan Agreement; and

(c)	the Lender will not treat the ownership realignment as an adverse event for the purposes of the Loan Agreement.

2.3	Share Cancellation and Reissue Waiver

The Lender irrevocably waives any right to treat the following as a breach of the Loan Agreement or as triggering any rights or remedies under the Loan Agreement:

(a)	the cancellation of the Borrower’s existing shares (including the 100 Class B shares held by CBS);

(b)	the issue of new shares in the Borrower (including the 4,000 Common Shares issued to CBS, being 40,000 Common Shares after the Share Split);

(c)	the 10-for-1 share split; and

(d)	the adoption of the amended and restated constitution (V3.1).

2.4	Constitution Change Waiver

The Lender acknowledges that the adoption of the amended and restated constitution as part of the Recapitalisation does not:

(a)	adversely affect the Lender’s rights under the Loan Agreement;

(b)	adversely affect the Security; or

(c)	trigger any rights or remedies under the Loan Agreement.

3.	WAIVERS AND VARIATIONS — SERIES A

3.1	Series A and Subsequent Equity Rounds — Permanent Waiver

The Lender irrevocably and unconditionally waives any right to:

(a)	treat the Series A or any subsequent bona fide equity financing approved by the Board as a “change of control”, “change of ownership”, or similar event under the Loan Agreement;

(b)	declare an Event of Default, Review Event, or similar event under the Loan Agreement as a result of any such equity financing;

(c)	accelerate, demand early repayment of, or otherwise enforce the Loan Agreement as a result of any such equity financing; or

(d)	exercise any other right or remedy under the Loan Agreement that would otherwise be triggered by any such equity financing.

For the avoidance of doubt:

(e)	This waiver is unconditional and applies regardless of the resulting ownership or voting structure of the Borrower following completion of the Series A or any subsequent equity financing.

(f)	The Lender’s rights under the Loan Agreement will not revive by reason of any change in the Borrower’s ownership or voting structure occurring at or after completion of the Series A.

(g)	This waiver extends to any follow-on equity rounds, convertible note conversions, ESOP exercises, or other equity issuances approved by the Board after the Series A.

3.2	Negative Pledge Carve-Out — Series A Priority

The Lender agrees that any Negative Pledge in the Loan Agreement is varied to permit the Borrower to grant security interests (each a Permitted Security Interest) in favour of:

(a)	any Series A Investor or any security trustee or nominee acting on behalf of Series A Investors, to the extent required by the terms of the Series A or reasonably requested by Series A Investors; and

(b)	any bank or financial institution providing senior debt financing to the Borrower, provided that such financing is approved by the Board,

provided that, in each case:

(c)	any security granted to persons described in clause 3.2(a) or (b) ranks ahead of the Security, unless the Lender agrees in writing to a different ranking; and

(d)	the Lender will, upon request by the Borrower or any Series A Investor, execute such subordination deeds, intercreditor agreements, or other documents as are reasonably required to give effect to the priority described in clause 3.2(c).

3.3	Subordination to Series A

The Lender agrees that, from completion of the Series A until the Loan Agreement has been repaid in full and all Security released:

(a)	all principal, interest, fees, costs, and other amounts owing to the Lender under or in connection with the Loan Agreement are subordinated in right of payment to all amounts owing to any Series A Investor or holder of preferred shares issued in the Series A;

(b)	the Lender will not, without the prior written consent of the Board (including, if appointed, at least one director nominated by Series A Investors):

(i)	demand or accept any repayment of principal or interest (other than the mandatory repayment contemplated by clause 6);

(ii)	take any enforcement action in respect of the Loan Agreement or the Security;

(iii)	exercise any rights as a secured creditor; or

(iv)	commence or threaten any legal proceedings against the Borrower;

(c)	in any liquidation, administration, or insolvency of the Borrower, the Lender will not receive any distribution or payment until all amounts owing to Series A Investors have been paid in full; and

(d)	the Lender acknowledges that the intent of this clause is to ensure that Series A Investors are not exposed to any credit risk, security dilution, or enforcement risk arising from the existence of the Loan Agreement or the Security.

3.4	Preferred Share Rights

The Lender acknowledges that the Series A will involve the issue of preferred shares with rights that rank ahead of the Common Shares held by CBS, including:

(a)	liquidation preferences;

(b)	anti-dilution protections;

(c)	dividend preferences;

(d)	redemption rights;

(e)	conversion rights; and

(f)	class voting rights,

and agrees that the grant of such rights does not constitute a breach of the Loan Agreement or trigger any rights or remedies under the Loan Agreement.

4.	VARIATIONS TO LOAN AGREEMENT

4.1	Change of Control Definition

If the Loan Agreement contains a definition of “change of control”, “change of ownership”, or similar term, that definition is varied to exclude:

(a)	the Recapitalisation; and

(b)	the Series A and any subsequent bona fide equity financing approved by the Board.

4.2	Ownership Covenant

If the Loan Agreement contains any covenant relating to the ownership structure of the Borrower, that covenant is varied to:

(a)	reflect the post-Recapitalisation ownership structure (96% CobaltBlu / 4% CBS); and

(b)	permit the Series A and any subsequent changes to the Borrower’s ownership structure resulting from bona fide equity financings approved by the Board.

4.3	Negative Pledge Variation

Any Negative Pledge in the Loan Agreement is varied to permit Permitted Security Interests as set out in clause 3.2.

4.4	No Other Variations

Except as expressly set out in this Deed, the Loan Agreement is not varied and remains in full force and effect until repayment in accordance with clause 6.

5.	CONFIRMATIONS

5.1	Loan Agreement Status

The Lender and the Borrower confirm that:

(a)	the Loan Agreement remains in full force and effect following the Recapitalisation, subject to the waivers, variations, and subordination provisions set out in this Deed;

(b)	as at the date of this Deed, the amount outstanding under the Loan Agreement is approximately A$209,000 (principal and accrued interest), with the exact amount to be confirmed prior to Series A completion;

(c)	the Security remains binding as between the Lender and the Borrower; and

(d)	neither party is in breach of the Loan Agreement as at the date of this Deed.

5.2	No Default

The Lender confirms that, as at the date of this Deed:

(a)	no Event of Default has occurred and is continuing under the Loan Agreement; and

(b)	the Lender is not aware of any circumstances that would, with the giving of notice or lapse of time, constitute an Event of Default.

5.3	Security Confirmation and Limitation

The Borrower confirms that:

(a)	the security interests granted in favour of the Lender under the Loan Agreement remain binding as between the Borrower and the Lender;

(b)	the Recapitalisation does not affect the validity of the Security as between the parties;

(c)	the Borrower makes no representation as to the perfection or priority of the Security against third parties, and the parties acknowledge that the Security has not been registered on the Personal Property Securities Register (PPSR) and is therefore unperfected; and

(d)	as at the date of this Deed, the Borrower is not aware of any third party that has acquired rights in respect of the collateral that would adversely affect the ability of the Borrower and the Lender to give full effect to the discharge and release contemplated by clause 6.4.

5.4	Series A Disclosure

The Borrower confirms that it will disclose the existence of this Deed, the Loan Agreement, and the Security to prospective Series A Investors as part of the due diligence process, and that the Lender consents to such disclosure.

6.	MANDATORY REPAYMENT AT SERIES A

6.1	Binding Commitment to Repay

Upon completion of the Series A, the Borrower must apply part of the Series A proceeds to repay in full all amounts outstanding under the Loan Agreement (including all principal, accrued interest, fees, and costs), such repayment to occur on or immediately prior to completion of the Series A.

For the avoidance of doubt, this is a binding obligation on the Borrower and is not subject to any conditions relating to working capital requirements or restrictions imposed by Series A Investors.

6.2	Condition Precedent to Series A

The Lender and the Borrower acknowledge and agree that:

(a)	full repayment of the Loan Agreement and release of all Security in accordance with this clause 6 is intended to be a condition precedent to completion of the Series A;

(b)	the Borrower will include this condition in the Series A subscription agreement or term sheet; and

(c)	the Lender will cooperate with the Borrower and Series A Investors to ensure that the repayment and discharge can occur simultaneously with or immediately prior to Series A funds being received by the Borrower.

6.3	Prepayment Terms

In respect of the prepayment contemplated by this clause 6:

(a)	the Borrower must give the Lender at least 5 Business Days’ notice of the expected Series A completion date and the prepayment amount;

(b)	no prepayment penalty, break cost, or early repayment fee will be payable by the Borrower;

(c)	upon receipt of the prepayment amount, the Lender must, within 1 Business Day, release the Security to the extent of the prepayment; and

(d)	if the prepayment is of the full amount outstanding, the Lender must execute and deliver the documents described in clause 6.4.

6.4	Full Discharge and Release

Upon receipt of full repayment of all amounts outstanding under the Loan Agreement at Series A close, the Lender will, within 2 Business Days, execute and deliver to the Borrower:

(a)	a deed of discharge and release in a form reasonably required by the Borrower or Series A Investors, confirming:

(i)	receipt of full repayment of all amounts owing under the Loan Agreement;

(ii)	discharge of all obligations, covenants, and undertakings under the Loan Agreement;

(iii)	release and discharge of all Security and any other security interests granted by the Borrower in favour of the Lender; and

(iv)	confirmation that the Lender has no further rights, claims, or remedies against the Borrower under or in connection with the Loan Agreement;

(b)	all documents necessary to remove or procure the removal of any PPSR registrations in relation to the Security (if applicable), including executed PPSR financing change statements; and

(c)	any other documents or confirmations reasonably requested by the Borrower, Series A Investors, or their legal advisors to evidence the full and final discharge of the Loan Agreement and Security.

6.5	Lender Cooperation

The Lender agrees to:

(a)	cooperate with the Borrower and Series A Investors to facilitate the orderly repayment and discharge of the Loan Agreement at Series A close;

(b)	make itself available (including through its authorised representative Jim Ellwood) to execute documents and provide confirmations as required during the Series A closing process; and

(c)	not take any action that would delay, impede, or frustrate the completion of the Series A or the repayment and discharge contemplated by this clause 6.

7.	REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES

7.1	Borrower Representations

The Borrower represents and warrants to the Lender that:

(a)	it has full power and authority to enter into and perform its obligations under this Deed;

(b)	this Deed constitutes a legal, valid, and binding obligation of the Borrower, enforceable in accordance with its terms;

(c)	the execution and performance of this Deed does not breach any law, regulation, order, or agreement to which the Borrower is a party;

(d)	all representations and warranties given by the Borrower under the Loan Agreement remain true and correct as at the date of this Deed; and

(e)	no Event of Default has occurred and is continuing.

7.2	Lender Representations

The Lender represents and warrants to the Borrower that:

(a)	it has full power and authority to enter into and perform its obligations under this Deed;

(b)	this Deed constitutes a legal, valid, and binding obligation of the Lender, enforceable in accordance with its terms;

(c)	the execution and performance of this Deed does not breach any law, regulation, order, or agreement to which the Lender is a party;

(d)	all persons who have signed this Deed on behalf of the Lender have been duly authorised to do so by the CBS board on 16 January 2026, with Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstaining from all votes relating to this Deed; and

(e)	the Lender acknowledges that this Deed is entered into for the benefit of prospective Series A Investors and that Series A Investors may rely on the waivers, subordination provisions, and repayment commitments set out in this Deed.

8.	GENERAL PROVISIONS

8.1	Entire Agreement

This Deed, together with the Loan Agreement and the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed between the Lender, the Borrower, and CobaltBlu Pty Ltd, constitutes the entire agreement between the parties in relation to its subject matter.

8.2	Amendment

This Deed may only be amended by a written document signed by both parties. For the avoidance of doubt, once the Series A has completed, no amendment to clauses 3, 6, or Annexure A may be made without the prior written consent of the Board (including, if appointed, at least one director nominated by Series A Investors).

8.3	Waiver

A waiver of any right under this Deed is only effective if it is in writing and signed by the party granting the waiver.

8.4	Severability

If any provision of this Deed is invalid or unenforceable, it will be severed from this Deed and the remaining provisions will continue in full force and effect.

8.5	Counterparts

This Deed may be executed in any number of counterparts (including electronic counterparts), each of which is an original and all of which together constitute one instrument.

8.6	Governing Law

This Deed is governed by the laws of New South Wales, Australia.

8.7	Jurisdiction

Each party irrevocably submits to the non-exclusive jurisdiction of the courts of New South Wales and courts of appeal from them.

8.8	Costs

Each party bears its own costs in connection with the negotiation, preparation, and execution of this Deed.

8.9	Further Assurances

Each party must do all things and execute all documents necessary or desirable to give full effect to this Deed.

8.10	Third Party Beneficiaries

The parties acknowledge and agree that the waivers, variations, subordination provisions, and repayment commitments set out in this Deed are intended to benefit prospective Series A Investors, and that Series A Investors may enforce those provisions against the Lender as third party beneficiaries under applicable law.

9.	EXECUTION

EXECUTED as a deed.

SIGNED, SEALED AND DELIVERED by CBS GROUP PTY LTD ACN 164 870 080 in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth):

Note: Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstained from this resolution due to his interests in Water Roads Pty Ltd and CobaltBlu Pty Ltd.

SIGNED, SEALED AND DELIVERED by WATER ROADS PTY LTD ACN 686 900 014 in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth):

ANNEXURE A — SUMMARY OF WAIVERS AND VARIATIONS

ANNEXURE B — SERIES A INVESTOR PROTECTIONS SUMMARY

This Annexure summarises the key protections provided to Series A Investors under this Deed.

1.	Permanent Waiver of Change of Control Rights

CBS has unconditionally and irrevocably waived all change of control, ownership restructuring, and related rights under the Loan Agreement in respect of the Series A and all future equity rounds (clause 3.1). These rights will not revive regardless of the post-Series A ownership structure. The waiver is not subject to any thresholds for CobaltBlu ownership or limits on investor shareholdings.

2.	Structural Subordination

All amounts owing to CBS under the Loan Agreement are subordinated in right of payment to all amounts owing to Series A Investors (clause 3.3(a)). CBS cannot demand repayment, take enforcement action, or exercise secured creditor rights without Board consent including Series A director consent (clause 3.3(b)). In any insolvency, CBS receives nothing until Series A Investors are paid in full (clause 3.3(c)).

3.	Security Priority

Any security granted to Series A Investors ranks ahead of CBS’s Security (clause 3.2(c)). CBS is required to execute subordination deeds and intercreditor agreements as reasonably requested (clause 3.2(d)). CBS’s Security is unperfected (no PPSR registration) and will be fully released at Series A close (clauses 5.3(c) and 6.4).

4.	Mandatory Repayment at Close

Water Roads is legally obligated to repay the CBS loan in full at Series A close (clause 6.1). Full repayment and discharge is a condition precedent to Series A completion (clause 6.2). CBS must provide a comprehensive discharge and release within 2 Business Days of receiving repayment (clause 6.4).

5.	No Prepayment Penalties

No prepayment penalty, break cost, or early repayment fee applies to the Series A repayment (clause 6.3(b)).

6.	Lender Cooperation Obligations

CBS is obligated to cooperate with Series A closing, including making Jim Ellwood available to execute documents (clause 6.5). CBS may not take any action that would delay or frustrate Series A completion (clause 6.5(c)).

7.	Third Party Beneficiary Rights

Series A Investors may enforce the protections in this Deed as third party beneficiaries (clause 8.10).

8.	Amendment Restrictions

Once the Series A has completed, key investor protection clauses (clauses 3, 6, and this Annexure) may not be amended without Series A director consent (clause 8.2).

Net Effect for Series A Investors

The CBS loan presents zero credit risk, zero security dilution risk, and zero governance interference risk to Series A Investors because: (1) it will be fully repaid and discharged at Series A close; (2) if for any reason repayment is delayed, CBS is structurally subordinated and cannot take any action without Series A director consent; (3) CBS has permanently waived all change of control and related rights; and (4) any Series A security ranks ahead of CBS’s unperfected security.

END OF DEED

The Directors

Attention: Sarah Margaret Taylor, Director and Company Secretary

Re: Recapitalisation — Transmittal of Executed CBS Documents

Dear Sarah,

I write in my capacity as independent director of CBS Group Pty Ltd (CBS) and chair of the CBS board to transmit the enclosed documents in connection with the recapitalisation of Water Roads Pty Ltd (the Recapitalisation).

1. Enclosed Documents

The following documents, duly executed by CBS, are enclosed with this letter:

2. Authority

The execution of each of the documents listed at items 1–3 above was authorised by written resolutions of the directors of CBS dated 16 January 2026 (the January Resolutions), passed pursuant to section 248A of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth). The January Resolutions were approved by me as the sole disinterested director, with Jeffrey Alan Dusting present but abstaining from all votes due to his material personal interests in Water Roads and CobaltBlu Pty Ltd.

The adoption of the CBS Conflict of Interest Policy V6.0 (item 4) was resolved at the CBS board meeting of 5 February 2026, again with my approval as the sole voting director and Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstaining.

3. Manner of Execution

Documents 1–3 have been executed by CBS in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), by the signatures of:

(a) Jim Ellwood, as director; and

(b) [INSERT SECOND SIGNATORY — Jeff Dusting as director / company secretary, or sole director if applicable].

Jeffrey Alan Dusting’s signature as a second s127 signatory (where applicable) is for the purpose of formal execution validity only. The substantive approval of all CBS decisions was given by me as the sole disinterested director, as recorded in the January Resolutions.

4. Conflict Management Confirmation

I confirm the following in relation to the conflict of interest framework applicable to the enclosed documents:

(a) Jeffrey Alan Dusting disclosed his material personal interests in Water Roads and CobaltBlu by Standing Notice under section 192 of the Act dated 1 January 2026, tabled at the CBS board meeting of 16 January 2026 and confirmed at the meeting of 5 February 2026;

(b) Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstained from voting on all resolutions authorising the execution of these documents;

(c) I, as the sole disinterested director, approved all decisions relating to CBS’s participation in the Recapitalisation, including the consents, waivers, subordination, and loan variation arrangements set out in the enclosed deeds;

(d) the CBS board has adopted the CBS Conflict of Interest Policy V6.0 (Institutional), which establishes an ongoing framework for managing the conflicts arising from Jeffrey Alan Dusting’s cross-directorships and the Taylor–Dusting family interests; and

(e) I am satisfied that the conflict management procedures followed by CBS (disclosure, abstention, independent approval, documented rationale) are appropriate for the nature and complexity of the Recapitalisation.

5. Commercial Rationale

For the avoidance of doubt, I confirm that in approving CBS’s entry into each of the enclosed documents, I was satisfied that doing so was in CBS’s commercial interests, having regard to:

(a) the correction of Historic Defects in Water Roads’ capital structure and alignment with the Agreed Ownership of 96% CobaltBlu / 4% CBS;

(b) the mandatory repayment of the CBS Loan (approximately A$209,000 outstanding) in full from Series A proceeds at close;

(c) the necessity of the subordination and waiver arrangements to facilitate a Series A financing, which will provide Water Roads with the capital to execute its business plan and thereby protect CBS’s equity value; and

(d) the preservation of CBS’s 4.00% equity interest in Water Roads on terms that are fair and reasonable in the circumstances.

6. Investor Data Room

CBS consents to copies of the enclosed documents (including the Conflict of Interest Policy) being placed in the Water Roads investor data room for the purposes of Series A due diligence. I am available to meet with prospective investors to discuss CBS’s governance framework and the conflict management arrangements summarised above.

7. Requests

Please arrange for:

(a) fully executed counterparts of documents 1–3 to be returned to CBS for filing in our minute book;

(b) confirmation that the ASIC lodgements required by the Recapitalisation Deed have been completed (or are in progress); and

(c) confirmation of the current loan balance outstanding under the Secured Loan Agreement dated 31 August 2025, including accrued interest to date, to allow CBS to prepare the discharge documentation in advance of Series A close.

Please do not hesitate to contact me if you require anything further from CBS in connection with the Recapitalisation or the Series A financing.

Yours sincerely,

CBS Group Pty Ltd — Transmittal Letter — Recapitalisation Documents — Confidential

### WaterRoads_Recapitalisation_Deed_V7_EXECUTION_READY.docx

RECAPITALISATION DEED

Version 7 — Final Aligned

WATER ROADS PTY LTD

ACN 686 900 014

DATE: 15 January 2026

CONFIDENTIAL

Changes from V6.1: CBS Loan date changed to placeholder (was hardcoded “1 August 2025”, needs verification against Loan Variation V7 which flags 1 Aug vs 31 Aug). Schedule 2 and 3 notes updated to reflect CBS Consent V7 and CBS Loan Variation V7 now exist. CBS execution block updated with abstention/independent director note for consistency with CBS Consent V7 and Loan Variation V7. No substantive legal content changed.

Changes from V5 (in V6.1): Board date corrected (14→15 Jan). Share numbers confirmed at 100K pre-split / 1M post-split (matching original V5). CBS deed dates changed to placeholders. Constitution reference updated to V3.1. Conflict disclosure framework added (clause 7). CobaltBlu address to be verified.

PARTIES

WATER ROADS PTY LTD ACN 686 900 014 of Unit 142, 19 Hickson Road, Dawes Point NSW 2000 (Company)

COBALTBLU PTY LTD ACN 103 595 071 of [INSERT COBALTBLU ADDRESS — verify against ASIC extract] (CobaltBlu)

CBS GROUP PTY LTD ACN 164 870 080 of [INSERT CBS ADDRESS — verify against ASIC extract] (CBS)

(CobaltBlu and CBS together, the Shareholders)

RECITALS

A.	The Company was incorporated on 8 May 2025 as an Australian proprietary company limited by shares.

B.	As at the date of this Deed, the Company has on issue:

(i)	1,000 shares described on the ASIC register as “FOU” or “FOUNDER’S” shares, held by CobaltBlu; and

(ii)	100 shares described on the ASIC register as “CLASS B” shares, held by CBS,

(together, the Existing Shares).

C.	The Company’s historic capital structure contains procedural and documentation defects, including:

(i)	mismatch between the ASIC register class codes and the Company’s constitution;

(ii)	sequencing issues in relation to prior share issuances;

(iii)	authority defects in relation to share issuances made under CEO delegation;

(iv)	misalignment between the agreed economic deal between the Shareholders and the recorded ownership percentages; and

(v)	inconsistency between the constitution’s share class framework and the intended capital structure,

(together, the Historic Defects).

D.	The Shareholders have agreed that the intended economic arrangement between them is:

(i)	CobaltBlu: 96% of the Company’s issued share capital; and

(ii)	CBS: 4% of the Company’s issued share capital,

(the Agreed Ownership).

E.	The parties have agreed to implement a recapitalisation of the Company (the Recapitalisation) to:

(i)	cancel all Existing Shares;

(ii)	issue new shares in new share classes to achieve the Agreed Ownership;

(iii)	implement a share split to achieve a practical share count for Series A fundraising and ESOP purposes; and

(iv)	adopt an amended and restated constitution,

thereby creating a clean break in the Company’s chain of title and remedying the Historic Defects.

F.	The Shareholders have each consented to the Recapitalisation and waived any claims arising from the Historic Defects or the implementation of the Recapitalisation.

G.	The directors of the Company (Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting) are married to each other, are each directors and 50% shareholders of CobaltBlu, and Jeffrey Alan Dusting is also a director of CBS. Each director has given standing notices of interest under section 192 of the Corporations Act dated 1 January 2026, and has disclosed their interests at the board meeting of 15 January 2026 in reliance on section 194 of the Corporations Act (the Company being a proprietary company). CBS has obtained independent board approval for the Recapitalisation through Jim Ellwood as independent CBS director, with Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstaining from all CBS votes on the matter.

1.	DEFINITIONS AND INTERPRETATION

1.1	Definitions

In this Deed, unless the context otherwise requires:

“ASIC” means the Australian Securities and Investments Commission.

“Board” means the board of directors of the Company from time to time.

“Business Day” means a day that is not a Saturday, Sunday or public holiday in Sydney, New South Wales.

“CBS Consent and Waiver Deed” means the deed between the Company, CobaltBlu, and CBS in the form set out in Schedule 2, to be executed on or before the Completion Date.

“CBS Loan” means the secured loan facility provided by CBS to the Company pursuant to the loan agreement dated [INSERT LOAN DATE — verify: 1 August or 31 August 2025] between the Company and CBS, as varied by the CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed.

“CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed” means the deed between the Company and CBS in the form set out in Schedule 3, to be executed on or before the Completion Date.

“Common Shares” means ordinary shares in the capital of the Company designated as “Common Shares” having the rights set out in clause 5 of the New Constitution.

“Completion” means completion of the Recapitalisation in accordance with clause 4.

“Completion Date” means the date on which the last of the conditions precedent in clause 2.1 is satisfied or waived, or such other date as the parties agree in writing.

“Corporations Act” means the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth).

“Effective Time” means 11:59 pm (Sydney time) on the Completion Date.

“Existing Shares” has the meaning given in Recital B.

“F Shares” means ordinary shares in the capital of the Company designated as “F Shares” (Founder Shares) having the rights set out in clause 4 of the New Constitution, including the right to auto-convert into Common Shares upon a Qualifying Financing (as defined in the New Constitution).

“Historic Defects” has the meaning given in Recital C.

“New Constitution” means the amended and restated constitution of the Company in the form set out in Schedule 1 (being the Amended and Restated Constitution V3.1 effective 15 January 2026).

“New Shares” means:

(a)	96,000 F Shares to be issued to CobaltBlu; and

(b)	4,000 Common Shares to be issued to CBS,

pursuant to clause 3.2.

“Recapitalisation” has the meaning given in Recital E.

“Share Split” means the subdivision of each issued share in the Company into 10 shares of the same class pursuant to clause 3.3.

“Split Shares” means the shares on issue following the Share Split, being:

(a)	960,000 F Shares held by CobaltBlu; and

(b)	40,000 Common Shares held by CBS.

1.2	Interpretation

In this Deed, unless the context otherwise requires:

(a)	headings are for convenience only and do not affect interpretation;

(b)	the singular includes the plural and vice versa;

(c)	a reference to a party includes that party’s successors and permitted assigns;

(d)	a reference to a statute includes any amendment, consolidation or replacement of that statute;

(e)	a reference to a clause or Schedule is a reference to a clause of, or Schedule to, this Deed;

(f)	where a word or phrase is defined, other grammatical forms of that word or phrase have corresponding meanings;

(g)	a reference to “$” or “dollars” is a reference to Australian dollars; and

(h)	a reference to a document includes any variation or replacement of that document.

2.	CONDITIONS PRECEDENT

2.1	Conditions

Completion is conditional upon:

(a)	the Board having passed resolutions approving the Recapitalisation on 15 January 2026, including:

(i)	the cancellation of the Existing Shares;

(ii)	the creation of the F Shares and Common Shares classes;

(iii)	the issue of the New Shares;

(iv)	the Share Split;

(v)	the adoption of the New Constitution; and

(vi)	the lodgement of all necessary ASIC forms;

(b)	each director of the Company having disclosed any material personal interest in the Recapitalisation in accordance with sections 191 and 192 of the Corporations Act, including:

(i)	standing notices dated 1 January 2026 (tabled at the board meeting of 15 January 2026); and

(ii)	verbal disclosures at the board meetings of 15 January 2026 (WaterRoads) and 16 January 2026 (CBS),

with all directors voting in reliance on section 194 of the Corporations Act (the Company being a proprietary company);

(c)	the Shareholders having passed special resolutions approving:

(i)	the cancellation of the Existing Shares as a selective reduction of capital under section 256C of the Corporations Act;

(ii)	the issue of the New Shares;

(iii)	the Share Split under section 254H of the Corporations Act; and

(iv)	the adoption of the New Constitution under section 136 of the Corporations Act;

(d)	the directors of the Company having made a solvency declaration in accordance with section 256B(1) of the Corporations Act;

(e)	CBS having executed the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed in the form set out in Schedule 2;

(f)	CBS having executed the CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed in the form set out in Schedule 3; and

(g)	CobaltBlu having executed a shareholder consent in the form set out in Schedule 4.

2.2	Satisfaction of Conditions

The parties must use reasonable endeavours to satisfy the conditions in clause 2.1 as soon as practicable after the date of this Deed.

2.3	Waiver

A condition in clause 2.1 may only be waived in writing by all parties.

2.4	Long Stop Date

If the conditions in clause 2.1 are not satisfied or waived by 28 February 2026 (or such later date as the parties agree in writing) (Long Stop Date), any party may terminate this Deed by written notice to the other parties, and the parties will have no further obligations under this Deed other than obligations that have accrued before termination.

3.	RECAPITALISATION STEPS

3.1	Cancellation of Existing Shares

At the Effective Time, and subject to the satisfaction or waiver of the conditions in clause 2.1:

(a)	all Existing Shares are cancelled and cease to exist;

(b)	the rights attaching to the Existing Shares are extinguished;

(c)	the share classes to which the Existing Shares belonged (including any class described as “FOU”, “FOUNDER’S”, “Class A”, or “Class B”) are abolished; and

(d)	the Company’s share capital is reduced to zero.

3.2	Issue of New Shares

Immediately following the cancellation in clause 3.1:

(a)	the Company creates two new classes of shares:

(i)	F Shares (Founder Shares); and

(ii)	Common Shares,

each having the rights set out in the New Constitution;

(b)	the Company issues:

(i)	96,000 F Shares to CobaltBlu, credited as fully paid; and

(ii)	4,000 Common Shares to CBS, credited as fully paid;

(c)	the New Shares are issued for nil additional cash consideration, in recognition of the cancellation of the Existing Shares and the Shareholders’ agreement to the Recapitalisation; and

(d)	the Company’s issued share capital immediately following the issue of New Shares is 100,000 shares.

3.3	Share Split

Immediately following the issue of New Shares in clause 3.2:

(a)	each F Share is subdivided into 10 F Shares;

(b)	each Common Share is subdivided into 10 Common Shares;

(c)	the Company’s issued share capital immediately following the Share Split is 1,000,000 shares, comprising:

(i)	960,000 F Shares held by CobaltBlu (96%); and

(ii)	40,000 Common Shares held by CBS (4%); and

(d)	the rights attaching to each class of shares are unaffected by the Share Split.

3.4	Adoption of New Constitution

With effect from Completion:

(a)	the Company’s existing constitution (including the Deed of Amendment to Constitution dated 1 August 2025) is repealed in its entirety; and

(b)	the New Constitution (being the Amended and Restated Constitution V3.1, set out in Schedule 1) is adopted as the constitution of the Company.

3.5	Sequencing

The steps in clauses 3.1, 3.2, 3.3 and 3.4 occur in the order set out in this clause 3, and each step is conditional upon the completion of the preceding step. For the avoidance of doubt:

(a)	the cancellation of Existing Shares occurs first;

(b)	the issue of New Shares occurs immediately after the cancellation;

(c)	the Share Split occurs immediately after the issue of New Shares; and

(d)	the adoption of the New Constitution occurs simultaneously with Completion.

4.	COMPLETION

4.1	Time and Place

Completion takes place at 2:00 pm (Sydney time) on the Completion Date at the registered office of the Company, or at such other time and place as the parties agree in writing. Completion may occur by exchange of executed counterparts in electronic form.

4.2	Completion Actions

At Completion:

(a)	the Company must:

(i)	deliver to each Shareholder a share certificate for their Split Shares;

(ii)	update the Company’s share register to reflect the Split Shares;

(iii)	deliver to each Shareholder a copy of the post-Recapitalisation share register in the form set out in Schedule 5;

(iv)	deliver to each Shareholder a copy of the New Constitution; and

(v)	deliver to each Shareholder a copy of the board and shareholder resolutions passed pursuant to clause 2.1;

(b)	each Shareholder must:

(i)	deliver to the Company their existing share certificates (if any) for cancellation; and

(ii)	execute any documents reasonably required to give effect to the Recapitalisation.

4.3	ASIC Lodgement

Within 28 days after Completion, the Company must lodge with ASIC in sequential order:

(a)	Form 484 (Change to Company Details) — Step 1: notifying the cancellation of the Existing Shares (section C1), the post-cancellation share structure (section C3), and the updated members register (section C4);

(b)	Form 484 (Change to Company Details) — Step 2 (lodged after Step 1 is processed): notifying the issue of the New Shares (section C2), the post-issue share structure (section C3), and the updated members register (section C4);

(c)	Form 2205 (Notification of Share Split) — Step 3A (lodged after Step 2 is processed): notifying the 10-for-1 share split; and

(d)	Form 484 (Change to Company Details) — Step 3B (lodged with or immediately after Step 3A): notifying the post-split share structure (section C3) and the updated members register (section C4).

The Company must not lodge any subsequent step until the preceding step has been confirmed as processed by ASIC.

5.	REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES

5.1	Company Representations

The Company represents and warrants to each Shareholder that, as at the date of this Deed and at Completion:

(a)	it is a company duly incorporated and validly existing under the laws of Australia;

(b)	it has full power and authority to enter into and perform its obligations under this Deed;

(c)	this Deed constitutes a legal, valid and binding obligation of the Company, enforceable in accordance with its terms;

(d)	the execution and performance of this Deed does not breach any law, regulation, order, or agreement to which the Company is a party or by which it is bound;

(e)	the Existing Shares are the only shares on issue in the Company; and

(f)	there are no options, warrants, convertible securities, or other rights to acquire shares in the Company.

5.2	Shareholder Representations

Each Shareholder represents and warrants to the Company and the other Shareholder that, as at the date of this Deed and at Completion:

(a)	it is a company duly incorporated and validly existing under the laws of Australia;

(b)	it has full power and authority to enter into and perform its obligations under this Deed;

(c)	this Deed constitutes a legal, valid and binding obligation of that Shareholder, enforceable in accordance with its terms;

(d)	the execution and performance of this Deed does not breach any law, regulation, order, or agreement to which that Shareholder is a party or by which it is bound;

(e)	it is the sole legal and beneficial owner of the Existing Shares registered in its name, free from any encumbrance (other than the security interest granted under the CBS Loan);

(f)	it has received independent legal and financial advice in relation to this Deed and the Recapitalisation, or has had the opportunity to do so and has chosen not to; and

(g)	it enters into this Deed voluntarily and with full knowledge of its terms and consequences.

5.3	No Other Securities or Arrangements

Each Shareholder represents and warrants to the Company and the other Shareholder that, as at the date of this Deed and at Completion:

(a)	there are no warrants, options, convertible notes, simple agreements for future equity (SAFEs), or other instruments convertible into or exchangeable for shares in the Company;

(b)	there are no phantom equity, profit participation rights, or synthetic equity arrangements;

(c)	there are no side letters, supplemental agreements, or undisclosed arrangements that modify the economic terms of this Deed or the Agreed Ownership;

(d)	there are no most-favoured-nation (MFN) rights, ratchet provisions, or preferential rights granted to any person in respect of the Company’s securities;

(e)	there are no put options, call options, rights of first refusal, or other arrangements that would require the Company or any Shareholder to issue, transfer, or repurchase securities;

(f)	the Split Shares represent the entire issued share capital of the Company;

(g)	there are no agreements, understandings, or arrangements (written or oral) between any Shareholder and any third party that would alter the economic benefits or voting rights associated with the Split Shares; and

(h)	each Shareholder’s economic interest in the Company is accurately reflected by its percentage holding of Split Shares as set out in Schedule 5.

6.	RELEASES AND WAIVERS

6.1	Release of Historic Claims

Each Shareholder, for itself and its related bodies corporate, officers, employees, and agents:

(a)	releases and discharges the Company and its directors, officers, and employees from any and all claims, demands, actions, suits, or proceedings arising from or in connection with the Historic Defects;

(b)	releases and discharges the other Shareholder and its directors, officers, and employees from any and all claims, demands, actions, suits, or proceedings arising from or in connection with the Historic Defects; and

(c)	agrees not to make any claim against any person in respect of the Historic Defects.

6.2	Waiver of Pre-emptive Rights

Each Shareholder waives any pre-emptive rights, rights of first refusal, or similar rights it may have under the Company’s constitution or any shareholders’ agreement in respect of:

(a)	the cancellation of the Existing Shares;

(b)	the issue of the New Shares; and

(c)	the Share Split.

6.3	Waiver of Oppression Claims

Each Shareholder acknowledges and agrees that:

(a)	the Recapitalisation is fair and reasonable to all Shareholders;

(b)	the Recapitalisation does not constitute oppressive, unfairly prejudicial, or unfairly discriminatory conduct within the meaning of section 232 of the Corporations Act;

(c)	the reduction in CBS’s proportionate shareholding from 9.09% to 4.00% reflects the correction of a historical error to the Agreed Ownership, not a dilutive or prejudicial act; and

(d)	it will not make any application under Part 2F.1 of the Corporations Act in respect of the Recapitalisation.

7.	CONFLICT DISCLOSURE AND GOVERNANCE

7.1	Acknowledgement of Interests

The parties acknowledge that:

(a)	Sarah Margaret Taylor is a director and Company Secretary of the Company, a director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu, and the spouse of Jeffrey Alan Dusting;

(b)	Jeffrey Alan Dusting is a director of the Company, a director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu, a director of CBS, and the spouse of Sarah Margaret Taylor; and

(c)	each of Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting has a material personal interest in the Recapitalisation by reason of their interests described in paragraphs (a) and (b).

7.2	Disclosure and Compliance

The parties record that:

(a)	each director of the Company gave standing notices of interest under section 192 of the Corporations Act dated 1 January 2026, which were tabled at the board meeting of 15 January 2026;

(b)	each director verbally disclosed the nature and extent of their interests at the board meeting of 15 January 2026;

(c)	the directors voted on the Recapitalisation in reliance on section 194 of the Corporations Act (the Company being a proprietary company with only two directors, both of whom are interested);

(d)	Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstained from all votes at the CBS board meeting of 16 January 2026 relating to the Recapitalisation, CBS Consent and Waiver Deed, and CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed; and

(e)	Jim Ellwood, as independent CBS director, chaired the CBS board meeting of 16 January 2026 and has been authorised to execute all CBS-side documents in connection with the Recapitalisation.

7.3	Investor Disclosure

The parties agree that the conflict of interest framework described in this clause 7, including the spousal relationship, multi-directorship positions, and the governance measures adopted, will be fully disclosed in the Series A data room and investor materials.

8.	CLEAN BREAK

8.1	Effect of Recapitalisation

The parties acknowledge and agree that:

(a)	the Recapitalisation creates a clean break in the Company’s chain of title;

(b)	all securities currently on issue in the Company are the product of the Recapitalisation and the Share Split, implemented under the New Constitution, with unanimous Shareholder approval;

(c)	from the Effective Time onwards, the Company’s capital structure, share classes, and governance are clean, internally consistent, and aligned with Series A investment norms;

(d)	the Historic Defects relate only to instruments and transactions that have been superseded by this Deed; and

(e)	prospective investors may rely on this Deed as evidence of a clean and enforceable chain of title to the Company’s issued share capital.

8.2	Data Room Narrative

The parties agree that the following statement may be included in any investor data room or due diligence materials:

“The Company’s historic capital structure had procedural and drafting defects (see DD register), but those instruments have been superseded. All currently issued securities are the product of a single Recapitalisation and share split, implemented under a new constitution, with unanimous shareholder approval and properly documented consents and waivers (including CBS). From the Recapitalisation Effective Date onwards, the cap table, share classes and governance are clean, internally consistent, and aligned with Series A norms.”

9.	DIRECTORS’ SOLVENCY DECLARATION

9.1	Declaration

The directors of the Company declare that, in their opinion:

(a)	immediately after the Recapitalisation, there are reasonable grounds to believe that the Company will be able to pay its debts as and when they become due and payable; and

(b)	the Recapitalisation is fair and reasonable to all Shareholders and to prospective Series A investors.

9.2	Basis of Declaration

The declaration in clause 9.1 is made on the basis that:

(a)	the Recapitalisation does not involve any payment to Shareholders;

(b)	the Company’s assets and liabilities are unaffected by the Recapitalisation;

(c)	the Company’s creditors are not prejudiced by the Recapitalisation;

(d)	the directors have made reasonable inquiries into the Company’s financial position;

(e)	the Historic Defects identified in the due diligence risk register have been remediated through this Deed and the associated CBS deeds;

(f)	the Agreed Ownership (96% CobaltBlu / 4% CBS) reflects the original economic deal between the Shareholders;

(g)	CBS has provided informed consent and independent board approval (16 January 2026) to the Recapitalisation; and

(h)	the CBS Loan risk has been addressed through the CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed (carving out the Recapitalisation and Series A from restrictive covenants) and the binding commitment to discharge the CBS Loan in full upon receipt of repayment at Series A close.

10.	GENERAL PROVISIONS

10.1	Entire Agreement

This Deed, together with the Schedules, the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed, the CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed, and the New Constitution, constitutes the entire agreement between the parties in relation to the Recapitalisation and supersedes all prior agreements, understandings, and negotiations.

10.2	Amendment

This Deed may only be amended by a written document signed by all parties.

10.3	Waiver

A waiver of any right under this Deed is only effective if it is in writing and signed by the party granting the waiver.

10.4	Severability

If any provision of this Deed is invalid or unenforceable, it will be severed from this Deed and the remaining provisions will continue in full force and effect.

10.5	Counterparts

This Deed may be executed in any number of counterparts (including electronic counterparts), each of which is an original and all of which together constitute one instrument.

10.6	Governing Law

This Deed is governed by the laws of New South Wales, Australia.

10.7	Jurisdiction

Each party irrevocably submits to the non-exclusive jurisdiction of the courts of New South Wales and courts of appeal from them.

10.8	Costs

Each party bears its own costs in connection with the negotiation, preparation, and execution of this Deed.

10.9	Further Assurances

Each party must do all things and execute all documents necessary or desirable to give full effect to this Deed.

11.	EXECUTION

EXECUTED as a deed.

SIGNED, SEALED AND DELIVERED by WATER ROADS PTY LTD ACN 686 900 014 in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth):

SIGNED, SEALED AND DELIVERED by COBALTBLU PTY LTD ACN 103 595 071 in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth):

SIGNED, SEALED AND DELIVERED by CBS GROUP PTY LTD ACN 164 870 080 in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth):

Note: Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstained from all CBS board votes relating to this Deed due to his interests in Water Roads Pty Ltd and CobaltBlu Pty Ltd. This Deed was approved by independent CBS director Jim Ellwood.

## Cobalt Blu Board Meeting — January 2026


### CBU_Board_Paper_Resolutions_15Jan2026 (2).docx

*File: `CBU_Board_Paper_Resolutions_15Jan2026 (2).docx`*

BOARD PAPER AND RESOLUTIONS

Recapitalisation of Water Roads Pty Ltd — CobaltBlu Participation

1. Purpose and Agenda

This paper seeks CobaltBlu board and shareholder approvals for participation in the Recapitalisation of Water Roads Pty Ltd, in which CobaltBlu holds a 96% shareholding.

1.1 Agenda Items

2. Preliminary Matters

2.1 Standing Notices (Item 1)

The following Standing Notices under section 192 of the Corporations Act 2001 were tabled:

2.2 Section 194 Reliance (Item 2)

CobaltBlu is a proprietary company. Both directors have material personal interests in the Recapitalisation (each being a 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu). Pursuant to section 194 of the Corporations Act, both directors are entitled to vote on the matters being considered.

3. Recapitalisation — CobaltBlu Participation (Item 3)

3.1 Background

CobaltBlu is the majority shareholder of Water Roads Pty Ltd. The Recapitalisation will:

(a)  Cancel all existing shares in Water Roads (which may have Historic Defects)

(b)  Issue new shares to achieve the Agreed Ownership: CobaltBlu 96% / CBS 4%

(c)  Adopt Constitution V3.1 with properly constituted share classes

(d)  Implement a 10:1 share split

(e)  Create a 'clean break' in chain of title for Series A readiness

3.2 CobaltBlu Position

4. Shareholder Approval — Recapitalisation (Item 4)

4.1 Background

The Recapitalisation Deed requires unanimous shareholder consent from the shareholders of Water Roads. CobaltBlu, as the 96% shareholder, must provide its written consent.

4.2 Shareholder Consent V2 (Schedule 4 to Recap Deed)

The Shareholder Consent V2 confirms CobaltBlu's consent to:

(a)  The cancellation of all existing shares

(b)  The issue of new shares under Constitution V3.1

(c)  The 10:1 share split

(d)  The adoption of Constitution V3.1

(e)  The waiver of any claims arising from Historic Defects

5. Shareholder & Director Resolutions V3.0 (Item 5)

5.1 Background

The CobaltBlu Shareholder & Director Resolutions V3.0 (document reference R-01) is a combined resolutions document that records:

(a)  The board resolutions passed at this meeting

(b)  The shareholder resolutions consenting to the Recapitalisation

(c)  The authorisations for execution

This document will be filed in the Series A data room as evidence of CobaltBlu's corporate approvals.

6. Authorisation to Execute Documents (Item 6)

6.1 Documents Requiring Execution

7. Founder Protective Provisions (Item 7)

7.1 Background

Constitution V3.1 of Water Roads includes Founder Protective Provisions at clause 20, which attach to F Shares. As CobaltBlu will hold 960,000 F Shares (representing 96% of the Company), it is appropriate to note the protections this provides.

7.2 Summary of Founder Protective Provisions (Clause 20)

8. Summary of Resolutions

CERTIFIED as the resolutions passed at the Board Meeting held on 15 January 2026:

Date: 15 January 2026

ACN 103 595 071 |

### CBU_Board_Paper_s194_Declaration.docx

*File: `CBU_Board_Paper_s194_Declaration.docx`*

BOARD PAPER

Section 194 Proprietary Company Exception — Declaration and Reliance

1. Purpose

This paper documents the Board's reliance on section 194 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth) in relation to CobaltBlu's participation in the Recapitalisation of Water Roads Pty Ltd.

Both directors of CobaltBlu have material personal interests in the matters being considered — each is a 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu, which will hold 96% of Water Roads following the Recapitalisation. This paper explains the legal framework permitting interested directors to vote.

2. Legal Framework

2.1 Section 194 — The Proprietary Company Exception

In summary: Section 194 permits directors of proprietary companies to vote on matters in which they are interested, provided they have disclosed their interests as required by sections 191 and 192.

3. Application to CobaltBlu

3.1 Company Status

3.2 Director Interests

3.3 Disclosure — Standing Notices (s192)

4. Minute Entry — s194 Reliance

The following entry is to be recorded in the minutes of this meeting:

5. Recommendation

The Board is asked to:

(1)  NOTE that section 194 of the Corporations Act applies to CobaltBlu;

(2)  NOTE that both directors are entitled to vote on matters in which they are interested;

(3)  DIRECT that the s194 reliance be recorded in the minutes in the form set out in section 4 above.

___________________________

Sarah Margaret Taylor

Director

15 January 2026



| COBALTBLU PTY LTD
ACN 103 595 071 |



| Meeting: | Board Meeting CBU-2026-001 |

| Date: | 15 January 2026 |

| Paper Number: | CBU-2026-001-01 |

| Agenda Item: | 2 — Conflict of Interest Framework / s194 Reliance |

| Action Required: | For Noting — Record in Minutes |



| Corporations Act 2001 — Section 194
If:
(a)  a director of a proprietary company has a material personal interest in a matter that is being considered at a meeting of the company's directors; and
(b)  the director discloses the nature and extent of the interest and its relation to the affairs of the company as required by sections 191 and 192;
the director:
(c)  may be present while the matter is being considered at the meeting; and
(d)  may vote on the matter. |



| Company Type: | Proprietary company limited by shares |

| ACN: | 103 595 071 |

| Directors: | Sarah Margaret Taylor; Jeffrey Alan Dusting (2 directors, both interested) |

| Shareholders: | Sarah Margaret Taylor (50%); Jeffrey Alan Dusting (50%) |

| Relationship to WR: | 96% shareholder of Water Roads Pty Ltd (post-Recapitalisation) |

| s194 Eligible: | YES — proprietary company, not subsidiary of public company |



| Director | Material Personal Interests |

| Sarah Margaret Taylor | • 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu — benefits from confirmation of CobaltBlu's 96% WR stake
• Director of Water Roads Pty Ltd
• Married to Jeffrey Alan Dusting (fellow director and 50% shareholder) |

| Jeffrey Alan Dusting | • 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu — benefits from confirmation of CobaltBlu's 96% WR stake
• Director of Water Roads Pty Ltd and CBS Group Pty Ltd
• Married to Sarah Margaret Taylor (fellow director and 50% shareholder) |



| Director | Notice Date | Tabled | Document Ref |

| Sarah Margaret Taylor | 1 January 2026 | 15 January 2026 | N-03 |

| Jeffrey Alan Dusting | 1 January 2026 | 15 January 2026 | N-04 |



| MINUTE ENTRY — SECTION 194 RELIANCE
The Chair noted for the record that:
(a)  CobaltBlu Pty Ltd is a proprietary company limited by shares;
(b)  both directors of the Company have material personal interests in CobaltBlu's participation in the Recapitalisation of Water Roads Pty Ltd, each being a 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu;
(c)  CobaltBlu will hold 96% of Water Roads following the Recapitalisation, and both directors benefit from the confirmation of this holding on a clean chain of title;
(d)  each director has disclosed the nature and extent of their interest by giving a Standing Notice under section 192 of the Corporations Act dated 1 January 2026, tabled at this meeting;
(e)  each director has verbally disclosed their interests at the commencement of this meeting;
(f)  accordingly, pursuant to section 194 of the Corporations Act 2001, each director is entitled to be present while CobaltBlu's participation in the Recapitalisation is being considered at this meeting, and to vote on those matters;
(g)  the Board proceeds in reliance on section 194.
Both directors confirmed their understanding and intention to participate on that basis. |

### CobaltBlu_Observer_Invitation_Jim_Ellwood.docx

*File: `CobaltBlu_Observer_Invitation_Jim_Ellwood.docx`*

[INSERT DATE]

Mr Jim Ellwood

Director

CBS Group Pty Ltd

ACN 164 870 080

[INSERT ADDRESS]

Re: Invitation to Attend CobaltBlu Board Meeting as Observer

Dear Jim,

I write on behalf of the board of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (CobaltBlu) to invite you to attend the CobaltBlu board meeting scheduled for [INSERT DATE AND TIME] as an observer.

Background

As you know, CobaltBlu is the 96% shareholder of Water Roads Pty Ltd (Water Roads) and CBS Group Pty Ltd (CBS) holds the remaining 4%. You already attend Water Roads board meetings as an observer in your capacity as CBS independent director. We would like to extend a similar invitation for CobaltBlu’s board meetings, beginning with the February meeting.

The February meeting will cover the execution status of the Recapitalisation documents, acknowledgment of counterpart documents received from Water Roads and CBS, a detailed review of the Constitution V3.1 provisions affecting CobaltBlu, conflict management matters, and Series A readiness. The agenda and board pack will be provided to you in advance.

Purpose of the Invitation

CobaltBlu’s board comprises two directors — Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting — who are married to each other and are both directors of Water Roads. Unlike CBS, CobaltBlu does not have an independent director, and all decisions are made under section 194 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth) (the proprietary company exception).

Your attendance as an observer serves three purposes:

(a) CBS visibility. As CBS’s independent director, your presence gives CBS direct visibility into how CobaltBlu governs its Water Roads investment — which is relevant given the shared interests and cross-directorships across the three entities.

(b) Governance enhancement. Your presence provides an external perspective at a board that would otherwise operate without any independent voice. While you would have no obligation to intervene, your observations will be recorded in the minutes, creating an additional layer of accountability.

(c) Investor confidence. Series A investors conducting due diligence on the Water Roads cap table and related-party arrangements will see that the CBS independent director had line of sight across all three levels of the structure — Water Roads, CBS, and CobaltBlu. This strengthens the overall conflict management narrative.

Terms of Attendance

Your attendance is subject to the following terms, which mirror the arrangements for your observer attendance at Water Roads board meetings:

(a) You attend as an observer only. You will have no voting rights at CobaltBlu board meetings and will not be appointed as a director of CobaltBlu.

(b) The invitation is at CobaltBlu’s discretion and may be revoked at any time, without notice or reason. CobaltBlu may also exclude you from specific agenda items where the board considers your presence inappropriate (for example, matters involving a dispute between CobaltBlu and CBS).

(c) You owe no fiduciary duties to CobaltBlu. Your primary duties are to CBS. Nothing in this invitation creates a directorship, advisory relationship, or duty of care running from you to CobaltBlu or its shareholders.

(d) You may speak at the meeting if invited to do so by the chair. The agenda includes a standing item (“Observer’s comments”) for you to raise any observations or questions. Your comments will be recorded in the minutes.

(e) Board papers will be provided to you in advance of each meeting, subject to any confidentiality restrictions the board considers appropriate. You agree to treat all CobaltBlu board papers and discussions as confidential and not to disclose them to any person other than the CBS board (in your capacity as a CBS director).

(f) You may share relevant information from CobaltBlu board meetings with the CBS board to the extent reasonably necessary for CBS to discharge its governance obligations in relation to its Water Roads investment. CobaltBlu acknowledges that this information-sharing is a core purpose of the observer arrangement.

(g) This invitation does not create any right for CBS to appoint an observer or director to the CobaltBlu board. It is a voluntary governance arrangement that exists at CobaltBlu’s pleasure.

Meeting Details

Date: [INSERT DATE]

Time: [INSERT TIME]

Location: [INSERT — in person / video conference link]

Chair: Sarah Margaret Taylor

Board pack: Will be circulated to you by [INSERT DATE — recommend at least 3 business days before the meeting]

Acceptance

If you are willing to attend, please confirm by return email or by signing and returning a copy of this letter. If you have any questions about the terms of attendance, please don’t hesitate to call me.

We value your role in the governance framework across the Water Roads group structure and look forward to your participation.

Kind regards,

CobaltBlu Pty Ltd — Observer Invitation — Confidential



| COBALTBLU PTY LTD
ACN 103 595 071
[INSERT REGISTERED ADDRESS] |

PRIVATE AND CONFIDENTIAL

The Directors

Water Roads Pty Ltd

ACN 686 900 014

[INSERT ADDRESS]

Re: Recapitalisation — Transmittal of Executed CobaltBlu Documents

Dear Board,

I write in my capacity as director and company secretary of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (CobaltBlu) to transmit the enclosed documents in connection with the recapitalisation of Water Roads Pty Ltd (the Recapitalisation).

1. Enclosed Documents

The following documents, duly executed by CobaltBlu, are enclosed:

Note: Item 3 (Shareholder Consent V2) is intended to be attached as Schedule 4 of the Recapitalisation Deed V7. Please confirm it has been incorporated into the execution version.

2. Authority

CobaltBlu’s entry into the Recapitalisation Deed V7 (item 1) was authorised by:

(a) the CobaltBlu Shareholder & Director Resolutions V3.0 Institutional dated 15 January 2026, passed by both directors (Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting) acting under section 194 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth) (the Act), with both directors’ material personal interests fully disclosed via standing notices under section 192; and

(b) the CobaltBlu Shareholder Consent V2, signed by both shareholders (Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting, each holding 50% of CobaltBlu’s issued shares), authorising the Recapitalisation as it affects CobaltBlu’s shareholding in Water Roads.

The adoption of the CobaltBlu Conflict of Interest Policy V6.0 (item 4) was resolved by the CobaltBlu board on [INSERT DATE], again with both directors voting under s194 and all interests disclosed.

3. Manner of Execution

The Recapitalisation Deed V7 (item 1) has been executed by CobaltBlu in accordance with section 127 of the Act, by the signatures of:

(a) Sarah Margaret Taylor, as director; and

(b) Jeffrey Alan Dusting, as director.

4. Conflict Management Confirmation

I confirm the following in relation to the conflict of interest framework applicable to CobaltBlu’s decisions:

(a) CobaltBlu has two directors: Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting. Both are also directors of Water Roads (with Sarah serving as Company Secretary). Jeff is also a director of CBS Group Pty Ltd. Sarah and Jeff are married to each other and are each 50% shareholders of CobaltBlu.

(b) Both directors have material personal interests in the Recapitalisation by virtue of their directorships at Water Roads, their beneficial ownership of Water Roads shares through CobaltBlu, and their spousal relationship.

(c) CobaltBlu is a proprietary company. As both directors have interests in the relevant matters, CobaltBlu relies on section 194 of the Act (the proprietary company exception), which permits interested directors of a proprietary company to vote on matters in which they have a material personal interest, provided their interests have been disclosed under section 191 or 192.

(d) Both directors gave standing notices of interest under section 192 of the Act dated 1 January 2026. These notices were tabled at the CobaltBlu board meeting of [INSERT DATE] and cover all matters relating to the Recapitalisation and Series A financing.

(e) CobaltBlu has adopted the CobaltBlu Conflict of Interest Policy V6.0 (Institutional), which establishes an ongoing framework for managing the conflicts arising from the cross-directorship and family-interest structure. This policy is consistent with and complementary to the Water Roads COI Policy V6.0 and the CBS COI Policy V6.0.

(f) Jim Ellwood (independent director of CBS) has been invited to attend CobaltBlu board meetings as an observer, providing external visibility into CobaltBlu’s decision-making. His attendance at the February CobaltBlu board meeting will be recorded in the minutes.

(g) The CobaltBlu board has documented its commercial rationale for participating in the Recapitalisation in the V3.0 Resolutions and the February board pack. In summary, the Recapitalisation corrects Historic Defects in Water Roads’ capital structure, aligns the share register with the Agreed Ownership of 96% CobaltBlu / 4% CBS, and positions Water Roads for the Series A financing that is necessary to execute the business plan.

5. CobaltBlu’s Post-Recapitalisation Position

Following the Recapitalisation:

(a) CobaltBlu holds 960,000 F Shares in Water Roads (after the 10-for-1 share split), representing 96% of Water Roads’ issued share capital;

(b) CobaltBlu’s F Shares carry the Founder Protective Provisions under clause 20 of the Constitution V3.1, giving CobaltBlu effective veto rights over major structural decisions while it holds ≥30% on a Fully Diluted Basis;

(c) CobaltBlu retains the right to appoint one Founder Director under clause 16.2 while it holds ≥20% on a Fully Diluted Basis; and

(d) CobaltBlu’s F Shares will automatically convert to Common Shares upon a Qualifying Financing (clause 4.4), with the Founder Protective Provisions continuing based on percentage thresholds.

6. Series A Cooperation

CobaltBlu confirms its commitment to cooperate with Water Roads in connection with the proposed Series A equity financing, including:

(a) making directors available for investor meetings, presentations, and due diligence calls;

(b) providing CobaltBlu corporate information and governance documents as reasonably required for investor due diligence;

(c) negotiating in good faith the terms of a Shareholders Agreement, subject to CobaltBlu board approval of the final terms; and

(d) consenting to the placement of the enclosed documents (including the COI Policy) in the Water Roads investor data room.

7. Requests

Please arrange for:

(a) fully executed counterparts of the Recapitalisation Deed V7 to be returned to CobaltBlu for filing in our minute book;

(b) copies of the executed CBS documents (CBS Consent and Waiver Deed V7, CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed V7, and CBS Transmittal Letter) to be provided to CobaltBlu for our records;

(c) confirmation that the ASIC lodgements required by the Recapitalisation Deed have been completed or are in progress;

(d) confirmation of CobaltBlu’s updated shareholding on the Water Roads share register (960,000 F Shares / 96%); and

(e) notice of any Series A documentation timelines, so CobaltBlu can schedule board meetings for SHA approval as required.

Please don’t hesitate to contact me if you require anything further from CobaltBlu in connection with the Recapitalisation or Series A.

Yours sincerely,

CobaltBlu Pty Ltd — Transmittal Letter — Recapitalisation Documents — Confidential
