### Standing Notice Jeff CobaltBlu.docx

*File: `Standing Notice Jeff CobaltBlu.docx`*

STANDING NOTICE OF MATERIAL PERSONAL INTEREST

Section 192, Corporations Act 2001 (Cth)

To: The Directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (ACN 103 595 071)

From: Jeffrey Alan Dusting

Date: [●] February 2026

Re: Standing Notice of Material Personal Interest under section 192 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth)

1. NATURE OF INTERESTS

1.1 WaterRoads Directorship

I am a director of WaterRoads Pty Ltd (ACN 686 900 014) (WaterRoads). CobaltBlu is the holder of 1,000 Founder's Shares in WaterRoads, representing 90.91% of the issued share capital prior to the recapitalisation described in WaterRoads Board Resolutions WR‑2026‑000 to WR‑2026‑003 (the Recapitalisation), and will hold 96,000,000 F Shares (96.00%) following the Recapitalisation and share subdivision. As a director of WaterRoads, I owe duties to WaterRoads under sections 180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), which may conflict with my duties as a director of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (CobaltBlu or the Company).

1.2 CobaltBlu Beneficial Ownership

I hold a 50% beneficial interest in the issued share capital of CobaltBlu. The remaining 50% is held by my spouse, Sarah Margaret Taylor. I therefore have a direct beneficial interest in all shares held by CobaltBlu in WaterRoads, which increases from 90.91% to 96.00% under the Recapitalisation. The Recapitalisation benefits CobaltBlu (and therefore me personally) through the increase in CobaltBlu's proportionate shareholding in WaterRoads.

1.3 CBS Group Directorship

I am a director of CBS Group Pty Ltd (ACN 164 870 080) (CBS Group). CBS Group holds 100 Class B Shares in WaterRoads (9.09% pre‑Recapitalisation) and will hold 4,000,000 Common Shares (4.00%) following the Recapitalisation. CBS Group is also the lender under a Secured Loan Agreement dated 31 August 2025, providing a facility of up to A$500,000 secured over WaterRoads' assets. As a director of CBS Group, I owe duties to CBS Group under sections 180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), which may conflict with my duties as a director of CobaltBlu.

1.4 Spousal Relationship

I am the spouse of Sarah Margaret Taylor. Sarah Margaret Taylor is a director and the Company Secretary of WaterRoads, and a director and 50% beneficial owner of CobaltBlu. By reason of this spousal relationship, I have an interest in any matter that affects Sarah Margaret Taylor's interests as a director, officer, or beneficial owner of any entity that deals with CobaltBlu or in which CobaltBlu holds an interest.

2. EXTENT OF INTERESTS

Summary of conflict: I simultaneously owe duties to CobaltBlu (as its director and 50% beneficial owner), to WaterRoads (as its director), and to CBS Group (as its director). Where CobaltBlu is asked to consent to, approve, or facilitate any matter that affects its interests as the 96% majority shareholder of WaterRoads — including the Recapitalisation (which increases CobaltBlu's ownership from 90.91% to 96.00% while reducing CBS Group's from 9.09% to 4.00%), the CBS Group loan facility to WaterRoads, the Series A investment, and any transactions between CobaltBlu and WaterRoads or CBS Group — I have a material personal interest that may conflict with CobaltBlu's interests. My spousal relationship with Sarah Margaret Taylor further compounds this conflict, as Sarah has concurrent directorships at WaterRoads and CobaltBlu and 50% beneficial ownership of CobaltBlu.

3. MATTERS TO WHICH THIS NOTICE RELATES

This Standing Notice relates to, but is not limited to, the following matters considered by the CobaltBlu board:

(a) The Recapitalisation of WaterRoads, including the cancellation and reissuance of shares, adoption of the new WaterRoads Constitution (V3.2), share subdivision, and realignment of ownership percentages between CobaltBlu and CBS Group (WaterRoads Board Resolutions WR‑2026‑000 to WR‑2026‑003);

(b) Any transaction, arrangement, or dealing between CobaltBlu and WaterRoads, or which affects CobaltBlu's rights, interests, or obligations as a shareholder of WaterRoads;

(c) Any transaction, arrangement, or dealing between CobaltBlu and CBS Group, or any matter in which CBS Group's interests as minority shareholder and lender to WaterRoads may conflict with CobaltBlu's interests as majority shareholder;

(d) Any future issue, allotment, transfer, buyback, or cancellation of shares in WaterRoads, including Series A Preferred Shares and any shares issued on conversion of the CBS Group loan facility;

(e) The establishment, amendment, or administration of any employee equity or incentive plan at WaterRoads, including any grants to persons associated with CobaltBlu;

(f) Any dividend, distribution, or return of capital by WaterRoads;

(g) Any matter affecting CobaltBlu's rights as a shareholder of WaterRoads, including voting rights, pre‑emptive rights, information rights, drag‑along and tag‑along rights, and transfer restrictions;

(h) The Series A investment in WaterRoads, including negotiations with prospective investors, term sheet and investment agreement terms, board composition, and any matter in which the interests of CobaltBlu may diverge from the interests of WaterRoads, minority shareholders, or Series A Investors;

(i) Any potential sale, transfer, or encumbrance of CobaltBlu's shareholding in WaterRoads;

(j) Any matter in which CBS Group has a material interest by reason of its shareholding in or loan facility to WaterRoads, including any variation, waiver, repayment, discharge, or enforcement of the CBS Group loan facility;

(k) Any matter affecting Sarah Margaret Taylor's position as director, Company Secretary, or officer of WaterRoads, or her remuneration or equity grants from WaterRoads;

(l) Any related‑party transaction within the meaning of Chapter 2E of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth) involving WaterRoads, CBS Group, Sarah Margaret Taylor, or any entity controlled by or associated with any of them; and

(m) Any other matter in which the interests described in section 1 may reasonably be perceived to influence my judgment as a director of CobaltBlu.

4. POLICY ACKNOWLEDGMENTS AND DISINTERESTED DIRECTOR STATUS

I acknowledge that:

(a) This Standing Notice does not authorise me to act improperly or relieve me of my duties as a director of CobaltBlu under sections 180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth);

(b) I remain obliged to act in good faith in the best interests of CobaltBlu, to exercise care and diligence, and not to improperly use my position or information obtained as a director;

(c) I have received, read, and will comply with any conflict of interest policy adopted by CobaltBlu, including specific protocols relating to WaterRoads and CBS Group matters;

(d) By reason of my concurrent directorships of WaterRoads and CBS Group, my 50% beneficial ownership of CobaltBlu, and my spousal relationship with Sarah Margaret Taylor, I cannot be considered a disinterested director in respect of matters involving WaterRoads, CBS Group, or Sarah;

(e) Where CobaltBlu requires disinterested director approval for a transaction involving WaterRoads or CBS Group, such approval should be provided by a director who is independent of WaterRoads, CBS Group, myself, and Sarah Margaret Taylor;

(f) I will update this Standing Notice if the nature or extent of any interest disclosed above changes materially or if new interests arise that are not covered by this notice; and

(g) This Standing Notice extends to any matter in which the interests described in section 1 may reasonably be perceived to influence my judgment as a director.

5. DURATION AND TABLING

This Standing Notice remains in effect until:

(a) I notify the Board that an interest has ceased or materially changed; or

(b) I withdraw or vary this notice in writing.

Under section 192(3) of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), this Standing Notice must be tabled at the next directors' meeting after it is given. I request that this notice be tabled accordingly and recorded in the minutes of that meeting.

Signed:

...........................................................

Jeffrey Alan Dusting

Director, CobaltBlu Pty Ltd

Date: .......................................

For Company Secretary Use

END OF STANDING NOTICE

### Standing Notice Jeff CobaltBlu.pdf

STANDING NOTICE OF MATERIAL
PERSONAL INTEREST
Section 192, Corporations Act 2001 (Cth)
To: The Directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (ACN 103 595 071)
From: Jeffrey Alan Dusting

Date: [●] February 2026
Re: Standing Notice of Material Personal Interest under section 192 of the Corporations Act
2001 (Cth)


1. NATURE OF INTERESTS
1.1 WaterRoads Directorship
I am a director of WaterRoads Pty Ltd (ACN 686 900 014) (WaterRoads). CobaltBlu is the
holder of 1,000 Founder's Shares in WaterRoads, representing 90.91% of the issued share
capital prior to the recapitalisation described in WaterRoads Board Resolutions
WR‑2026‑000 to WR‑2026‑003 (the Recapitalisation), and will hold 96,000,000 F Shares
(96.00%) following the Recapitalisation and share subdivision. As a director of WaterRoads,
I owe duties to WaterRoads under sections 180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), which
may conflict with my duties as a director of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (CobaltBlu or the Company).

1.2 CobaltBlu Beneficial Ownership
I hold a 50% beneficial interest in the issued share capital of CobaltBlu. The remaining 50%
is held by my spouse, Sarah Margaret Taylor. I therefore have a direct beneficial interest in
all shares held by CobaltBlu in WaterRoads, which increases from 90.91% to 96.00% under
the Recapitalisation. The Recapitalisation benefits CobaltBlu (and therefore me personally)
through the increase in CobaltBlu's proportionate shareholding in WaterRoads.

1.3 CBS Group Directorship
I am a director of CBS Group Pty Ltd (ACN 164 870 080) (CBS Group). CBS Group holds 100
Class B Shares in WaterRoads (9.09% pre‑Recapitalisation) and will hold 4,000,000 Common
Shares (4.00%) following the Recapitalisation. CBS Group is also the lender under a Secured
Loan Agreement dated 31 August 2025, providing a facility of up to A$500,000 secured over
WaterRoads' assets. As a director of CBS Group, I owe duties to CBS Group under sections
180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), which may conflict with my duties as a director
of CobaltBlu.
1.4 Spousal Relationship
I am the spouse of Sarah Margaret Taylor. Sarah Margaret Taylor is a director and the
Company Secretary of WaterRoads, and a director and 50% beneficial owner of CobaltBlu.
By reason of this spousal relationship, I have an interest in any matter that affects Sarah
Margaret Taylor's interests as a director, officer, or beneficial owner of any entity that deals
with CobaltBlu or in which CobaltBlu holds an interest.

2. EXTENT OF INTERESTS

Summary of conflict: I simultaneously owe duties to CobaltBlu (as its director and 50%
beneficial owner), to WaterRoads (as its director), and to CBS Group (as its director). Where
CobaltBlu is asked to consent to, approve, or facilitate any matter that affects its interests
as the 96% majority shareholder of WaterRoads — including the Recapitalisation (which
increases CobaltBlu's ownership from 90.91% to 96.00% while reducing CBS Group's from
9.09% to 4.00%), the CBS Group loan facility to WaterRoads, the Series A investment, and
any transactions between CobaltBlu and WaterRoads or CBS Group — I have a material
personal interest that may conflict with CobaltBlu's interests. My spousal relationship with
Sarah Margaret Taylor further compounds this conflict, as Sarah has concurrent
directorships at WaterRoads and CobaltBlu and 50% beneficial ownership of CobaltBlu.

3. MATTERS TO WHICH THIS NOTICE RELATES
This Standing Notice relates to, but is not limited to, the following matters considered by the
CobaltBlu board:

(a) The Recapitalisation of WaterRoads, including the cancellation and reissuance of
shares, adoption of the new WaterRoads Constitution (V3.2), share subdivision, and
realignment of ownership percentages between CobaltBlu and CBS Group (WaterRoads
Board Resolutions WR‑2026‑000 to WR‑2026‑003);
(b) Any transaction, arrangement, or dealing between CobaltBlu and WaterRoads, or which
affects CobaltBlu's rights, interests, or obligations as a shareholder of WaterRoads;
(c) Any transaction, arrangement, or dealing between CobaltBlu and CBS Group, or any
matter in which CBS Group's interests as minority shareholder and lender to WaterRoads
may conflict with CobaltBlu's interests as majority shareholder;

(d) Any future issue, allotment, transfer, buyback, or cancellation of shares in WaterRoads,
including Series A Preferred Shares and any shares issued on conversion of the CBS Group
loan facility;
(e) The establishment, amendment, or administration of any employee equity or incentive
plan at WaterRoads, including any grants to persons associated with CobaltBlu;
(f) Any dividend, distribution, or return of capital by WaterRoads;

(g) Any matter affecting CobaltBlu's rights as a shareholder of WaterRoads, including voting
rights, pre‑emptive rights, information rights, drag‑along and tag‑along rights, and transfer
restrictions;
(h) The Series A investment in WaterRoads, including negotiations with prospective
investors, term sheet and investment agreement terms, board composition, and any
matter in which the interests of CobaltBlu may diverge from the interests of WaterRoads,
minority shareholders, or Series A Investors;
(i) Any potential sale, transfer, or encumbrance of CobaltBlu's shareholding in WaterRoads;

(j) Any matter in which CBS Group has a material interest by reason of its shareholding in
or loan facility to WaterRoads, including any variation, waiver, repayment, discharge, or
enforcement of the CBS Group loan facility;
(k) Any matter affecting Sarah Margaret Taylor's position as director, Company Secretary,
or officer of WaterRoads, or her remuneration or equity grants from WaterRoads;
(l) Any related‑party transaction within the meaning of Chapter 2E of the Corporations Act
2001 (Cth) involving WaterRoads, CBS Group, Sarah Margaret Taylor, or any entity
controlled by or associated with any of them; and

(m) Any other matter in which the interests described in section 1 may reasonably be
perceived to influence my judgment as a director of CobaltBlu.
4. POLICY ACKNOWLEDGMENTS AND DISINTERESTED
DIRECTOR STATUS
I acknowledge that:
(a) This Standing Notice does not authorise me to act improperly or relieve me of my duties
as a director of CobaltBlu under sections 180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth);

(b) I remain obliged to act in good faith in the best interests of CobaltBlu, to exercise care
and diligence, and not to improperly use my position or information obtained as a
director;
(c) I have received, read, and will comply with any conflict of interest policy adopted by
CobaltBlu, including specific protocols relating to WaterRoads and CBS Group matters;
(d) By reason of my concurrent directorships of WaterRoads and CBS Group, my 50%
beneficial ownership of CobaltBlu, and my spousal relationship with Sarah Margaret
Taylor, I cannot be considered a disinterested director in respect of matters involving
WaterRoads, CBS Group, or Sarah;

(e) Where CobaltBlu requires disinterested director approval for a transaction involving
WaterRoads or CBS Group, such approval should be provided by a director who is
independent of WaterRoads, CBS Group, myself, and Sarah Margaret Taylor;
(f) I will update this Standing Notice if the nature or extent of any interest disclosed above
changes materially or if new interests arise that are not covered by this notice; and
(g) This Standing Notice extends to any matter in which the interests described in section 1
may reasonably be perceived to influence my judgment as a director.

5. DURATION AND TABLING
This Standing Notice remains in effect until:
(a) I notify the Board that an interest has ceased or materially changed; or
(b) I withdraw or vary this notice in writing.

Under section 192(3) of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), this Standing Notice must be tabled
at the next directors' meeting after it is given. I request that this notice be tabled
accordingly and recorded in the minutes of that meeting.

STANDING NOTICE OF MATERIAL PERSONAL INTEREST

Section 192, Corporations Act 2001 (Cth)

To: The Directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (ACN 103 595 071)

From: Sarah Margaret Taylor

Date: [●] February 2026

Re: Standing Notice of Material Personal Interest under section 192 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth)

1. NATURE OF INTERESTS

1.1 WaterRoads Directorship

I am a director and the Company Secretary of WaterRoads Pty Ltd (ACN 686 900 014) (WaterRoads). CobaltBlu is the holder of 1,000 Founder's Shares in WaterRoads, representing 90.91% of the issued share capital prior to the recapitalisation described in WaterRoads Board Resolutions WR‑2026‑000 to WR‑2026‑003 (the Recapitalisation), and will hold 96,000,000 F Shares (96.00%) following the Recapitalisation and share subdivision. As a director and Company Secretary of WaterRoads, I owe duties to WaterRoads under sections 180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), which may conflict with my duties as a director of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd (CobaltBlu or the Company).

1.2 CobaltBlu Beneficial Ownership

I hold a 50% beneficial interest in the issued share capital of CobaltBlu. The remaining 50% is held by my spouse, Jeffrey Alan Dusting. I therefore have a direct beneficial interest in all shares held by CobaltBlu in WaterRoads, which increases from 90.91% to 96.00% under the Recapitalisation. The Recapitalisation benefits CobaltBlu (and therefore me personally) through the increase in CobaltBlu's proportionate shareholding in WaterRoads.

1.3 Spousal Relationship

I am the spouse of Jeffrey Alan Dusting. Jeffrey Alan Dusting is a director of WaterRoads, a director and 50% beneficial owner of CobaltBlu, and a director of CBS Group Pty Ltd (ACN 164 870 080) (CBS Group). CBS Group holds 100 Class B Shares in WaterRoads (9.09% pre‑Recapitalisation) and will hold 4,000,000 Common Shares (4.00%) following the Recapitalisation. CBS Group is also the lender under a Secured Loan Agreement dated 31 August 2025, providing a facility of up to A$500,000 secured over WaterRoads' assets. By reason of this spousal relationship, I have an interest in any matter that affects Jeffrey Alan Dusting's interests as a director, officer, or beneficial owner of any entity that deals with CobaltBlu or in which CobaltBlu holds an interest.

2. EXTENT OF INTERESTS

Summary of conflict: I simultaneously owe duties to CobaltBlu (as its director and 50% beneficial owner) and to WaterRoads (as its director and Company Secretary). Where CobaltBlu is asked to consent to, approve, or facilitate any matter that affects its interests as the 96% majority shareholder of WaterRoads — including the Recapitalisation (which increases CobaltBlu's ownership from 90.91% to 96.00% while reducing CBS Group's from 9.09% to 4.00%), the Series A investment, and any transactions between CobaltBlu and WaterRoads — I have a material personal interest that may conflict with CobaltBlu's interests. My spousal relationship with Jeffrey Alan Dusting further compounds this conflict, as Jeffrey has concurrent directorships at WaterRoads, CobaltBlu, and CBS Group.

3. MATTERS TO WHICH THIS NOTICE RELATES

This Standing Notice relates to, but is not limited to, the following matters considered by the CobaltBlu board:

(a) The Recapitalisation of WaterRoads, including the cancellation and reissuance of shares, adoption of the new WaterRoads Constitution (V3.2), share subdivision, and realignment of ownership percentages between CobaltBlu and CBS Group (WaterRoads Board Resolutions WR‑2026‑000 to WR‑2026‑003);

(b) Any transaction, arrangement, or dealing between CobaltBlu and WaterRoads, or which affects CobaltBlu's rights, interests, or obligations as a shareholder of WaterRoads;

(c) Any future issue, allotment, transfer, buyback, or cancellation of shares in WaterRoads, including Series A Preferred Shares and any shares issued on conversion of the CBS Group loan facility;

(d) The establishment, amendment, or administration of any employee equity or incentive plan at WaterRoads, including any grants to persons associated with CobaltBlu;

(e) Any dividend, distribution, or return of capital by WaterRoads;

(f) Any matter affecting CobaltBlu's rights as a shareholder of WaterRoads, including voting rights, pre‑emptive rights, information rights, drag‑along and tag‑along rights, and transfer restrictions;

(g) The Series A investment in WaterRoads, including negotiations with prospective investors, term sheet and investment agreement terms, board composition, and any matter in which the interests of CobaltBlu may diverge from the interests of WaterRoads, minority shareholders, or Series A Investors;

(h) Any potential sale, transfer, or encumbrance of CobaltBlu's shareholding in WaterRoads;

(i) Any matter in which Jeffrey Alan Dusting has a material personal interest by reason of his directorships at WaterRoads, CobaltBlu, or CBS Group;

(j) Any related‑party transaction within the meaning of Chapter 2E of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth) involving WaterRoads, CBS Group, Jeffrey Alan Dusting, or any entity controlled by or associated with any of them;

(k) Any matter affecting the CBS Group loan facility to WaterRoads, including any variation, waiver, repayment, discharge, or enforcement of that facility; and

(l) Any other matter in which the interests described in section 1 may reasonably be perceived to influence my judgment as a director of CobaltBlu.

4. POLICY ACKNOWLEDGMENTS

I acknowledge that:

(a) This Standing Notice does not authorise me to act improperly or relieve me of my duties as a director of CobaltBlu under sections 180–184 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth);

(b) I remain obliged to act in good faith in the best interests of CobaltBlu, to exercise care and diligence, and not to improperly use my position or information obtained as a director;

(c) I have received, read, and will comply with any conflict of interest policy adopted by CobaltBlu, including specific protocols relating to WaterRoads and CBS Group matters;

(d) By reason of my concurrent directorship and Company Secretary role at WaterRoads, my 50% beneficial ownership of CobaltBlu, and my spousal relationship with Jeffrey Alan Dusting, I cannot be considered a disinterested director in respect of matters involving WaterRoads, CBS Group, or Jeffrey;

(e) Where CobaltBlu requires disinterested director approval for a transaction involving WaterRoads or CBS Group, such approval should be provided by a director who is independent of WaterRoads, myself, and Jeffrey Alan Dusting;

(f) I will update this Standing Notice if the nature or extent of any interest disclosed above changes materially or if new interests arise that are not covered by this notice; and

(g) This Standing Notice extends to any matter in which the interests described in section 1 may reasonably be perceived to influence my judgment as a director.

5. DURATION AND TABLING

This Standing Notice remains in effect until:

(a) I notify the Board that an interest has ceased or materially changed; or

(b) I withdraw or vary this notice in writing.

Under section 192(3) of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), this Standing Notice must be tabled at the next directors' meeting after it is given. I request that this notice be tabled accordingly and recorded in the minutes of that meeting.

## Cobalt Blu Board Meeting — February 2026


### 05.1   CobaltBlu_ Recapitilisation Resolutions_V3_0_Institutional.docx

*File: `05.1   CobaltBlu_ Recapitilisation Resolutions_V3_0_Institutional.docx`*

COBALTBLU PTY LTD — SHAREHOLDER & DIRECTOR RESOLUTIONS (V3.0 INSTITUTIONAL)

COBALTBLU PTY LTD

ACN 103 595 071

WRITTEN RESOLUTIONS OF SHAREHOLDERS AND DIRECTORS

Pursuant to sections 249A and 248A of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth)

Date: [INSERT DATE — recommend executing on or before WaterRoads shareholder resolution date]

CONFIDENTIAL — BOARD PAPER

Changes from V2.0: Constitution clause cross-references corrected against V3.1 (conversion cl 4.3→4.4; Qualifying Financing definition cl 1.1→3.1; Reserved Matters list cl 20.1→20.2). Standing notice dates specified (1 January 2026). CBS board meeting date (16 January 2026) added. CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed V7 references added throughout. Background C (Recap Steps) completed. Document Control table updated. No substantive legal content changed.

PREAMBLE

The undersigned, being all of the shareholders and directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd ACN 103 595 071 (CobaltBlu or the Company), pass the following resolutions in writing pursuant to:

Section 249A of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth) (the Act) — shareholder resolutions passed without a meeting; and

Section 248A of the Act — director resolutions passed without a meeting.

These resolutions are effective when signed by all shareholders and all directors, and have the same effect as if passed at duly convened meetings of shareholders and directors respectively.

BACKGROUND AND CONTEXT

A. Current Shareholding and Investment

CobaltBlu holds 1,000 FOU/Founder's shares in WaterRoads Pty Ltd ACN 686 900 014 (WaterRoads or Portfolio Company), representing 90.91% of WaterRoads' issued share capital as at the date of these resolutions.

CobaltBlu's investment in WaterRoads represents the principal asset of CobaltBlu. The two directors and shareholders of CobaltBlu (Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting) also serve as directors of WaterRoads.

B. The Recapitalisation

WaterRoads proposes to implement a recapitalisation (the Recapitalisation) to correct historic defects in its capital structure and align the share register with the agreed ownership structure between CobaltBlu and CBS Group Pty Ltd ACN 164 870 080 (CBS Group).

The Recapitalisation is documented in:

(a) Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026 between WaterRoads, CobaltBlu, and CBS Group (the Recap Deed);

(b) CBS Consent and Waiver Deed dated [●] January 2026, to which CobaltBlu is or will become a party;

(c) CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed between WaterRoads and CBS Group (waiving loan covenants, subordinating the CBS Loan, and committing to full discharge at Series A close); and

(c) Amended and Restated Constitution of WaterRoads — Version 3.1 adopted by special resolution of WaterRoads shareholders effective 15 January 2026 (the New Constitution).

C. Recapitalisation Mechanics

The Recapitalisation involves the following sequential steps (collectively, the Recap Steps):

(i) the cancellation of all 1,100 Existing Shares (1,000 FOU/Founder’s shares held by CobaltBlu and 100 Class B shares held by CBS Group);

(ii) the issue of 100,000 new shares (96,000 F Shares to CobaltBlu and 4,000 Common Shares to CBS Group);

(iii) a 10-for-1 share split, increasing total share count to 1,000,000 (960,000 F Shares and 40,000 Common Shares); and

(iv) the adoption of the New Constitution (V3.1, effective 15 January 2026).

Agreed Ownership means the ownership structure agreed between CobaltBlu and CBS Group as documented in the Recap Deed, being 96.00% CobaltBlu and 4.00% CBS Group, and reflects the correction of Historic Defects (as defined in the Recap Deed).

D. Post-Recapitalisation Position

Following completion of the Recap Steps, CobaltBlu will hold:

960,000 F Shares in WaterRoads

Representing 96.00% of WaterRoads' issued share capital

Ranking in accordance with the New Constitution

E. Series A Financing and F Share Conversion

WaterRoads intends to pursue a Series A equity financing following the Recapitalisation. Key implications for CobaltBlu:

(a) Dilution: CobaltBlu's percentage shareholding will be diluted by the Series A issuance (expected quantum and terms to be determined by WaterRoads board in accordance with fiduciary duties and governance framework).

(b) F Share Conversion: Upon completion of a Qualifying Financing (as defined in clause 3.1 of the New Constitution — broadly, a bona fide equity financing of at least A$[●] on arms-length terms), CobaltBlu's F Shares will automatically convert into Common Shares on a 1:1 basis (clause 4.4 of the New Constitution).

(c) Founder Protections: While CobaltBlu (together with any other F Share holders, the F Share Majority) holds ≥30% of WaterRoads shares on a Fully Diluted Basis, certain Founder Protective Provisions apply (clause 20 of the New Constitution), requiring F Share Majority consent for specified major decisions.

(d) Board Representation: While the F Share Majority holds ≥20% on a Fully Diluted Basis, the F Share Majority has the right to appoint one Founder Director to the WaterRoads board (clause 16.2 of the New Constitution).

(e) Shareholders Agreement: Series A investors will require entry into a Shareholders Agreement, which may include further governance, consent, and exit provisions affecting CobaltBlu's rights as a shareholder.

F. CBS Consent and Waiver Deed

CBS Group (as WaterRoads' minority shareholder and secured lender) has consented to the Recapitalisation and waived certain rights. CobaltBlu is required to execute, or has been asked to be a party to, the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed to:

(a) acknowledge CBS Group's consent and the binding effect of the Recapitalisation;

(b) provide certain confirmations regarding the Agreed Ownership and Recap Steps; and

(c) undertake to comply with the governance framework set out in the New Constitution.

G. Governance Context

CobaltBlu is a proprietary company with two directors and two shareholders, each holding 50%:

Sarah Margaret Taylor — Director, Company Secretary, 50% shareholder

Jeffrey Alan Dusting — Director, 50% shareholder

Both are also directors of WaterRoads. Jeff is also a director of CBS Group. Jeffrey Alan Dusting abstained from all CBS votes on the Recapitalisation at the CBS board meeting of 16 January 2026, with Jim Ellwood (independent CBS director) authorised to execute all CBS-side documents.

CobaltBlu has adopted a Conflict of Interest — Board Policy (Version 6.0 – Institutional) which governs the management of conflicts arising from WaterRoads and CBS Group matters. The resolutions in this document are passed in accordance with that policy.

CONFLICT OF INTEREST DISCLOSURE

The directors make the following disclosures for the purposes of sections 191, 192, and 194 of the Act, and in accordance with CobaltBlu's Conflict of Interest Policy:

Material Personal Interests

(a) Sarah Margaret Taylor:

Director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu

Director and Company Secretary of WaterRoads

Director and 50% beneficial owner of CobaltBlu (which holds 90.91% pre-Recap / 96% post-Recap of WaterRoads)

Spouse of Jeffrey Alan Dusting

(b) Jeffrey Alan Dusting:

Director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu

Director of WaterRoads

Director of CBS Group Pty Ltd

Director and 50% beneficial owner of CobaltBlu (which holds 90.91% pre-Recap / 96% post-Recap of WaterRoads)

Spouse of Sarah Margaret Taylor

Nature of Conflict

Both directors have material personal interests in the resolutions below by virtue of:

(i) their roles as directors and 50% shareholders of CobaltBlu (the entity making the decisions);

(ii) their roles as directors of WaterRoads (the Portfolio Company subject to the Recapitalisation);

(iii) their beneficial ownership interests in WaterRoads through CobaltBlu's shareholding;

(iv) Jeff's additional role as a director of CBS Group (the counterparty to the Recap Deed and CBS Consent Deed); and

(v) their spousal relationship, which creates indirect interests in each other's positions.

Statutory Basis for Voting

CobaltBlu is a proprietary company with only two directors, both of whom are interested in these matters.

Section 194 of the Act permits directors of a proprietary company to vote on, and be present at a meeting to consider, a matter in which they have a material personal interest, provided:

the interest has been disclosed to the other directors in accordance with s191 or s192; and

the company is not a public company.

Reliance on s194: The directors resolve to vote on these resolutions in reliance on section 194, having made full disclosure as set out above.

Standing Notices

Both directors have given Standing Notices under section 192 of the Act, tabled at CobaltBlu board meetings, disclosing their ongoing interests in:

WaterRoads (directorship, shareholding via CobaltBlu)

CBS Group (Jeff's directorship)

Spousal relationship and indirect interests

Those Standing Notices remain in effect and cover all matters addressed in these resolutions.

Commercial Rationale

The directors are satisfied that, notwithstanding their conflicts:

(a) the Recapitalisation is in CobaltBlu's interests because it:

corrects Historic Defects in WaterRoads' capital structure;

aligns the share register with the Agreed Ownership of 96% CobaltBlu / 4% CBS;

facilitates WaterRoads' Series A financing, which is necessary for WaterRoads' business growth and the protection and enhancement of CobaltBlu's investment;

preserves CobaltBlu's majority position and Founder Protections under the New Constitution;

(b) the terms of the Recapitalisation (including the share-for-share exchange, nil cash consideration, and adoption of the New Constitution) are fair and reasonable to CobaltBlu;

(c) the Series A financing (while dilutive in percentage terms) is necessary for WaterRoads to execute its business plan and represents the most commercially viable path to value creation for CobaltBlu as a shareholder;

(d) CobaltBlu's participation in the CBS Consent Deed is necessary to implement the Recapitalisation and does not involve CobaltBlu giving up material rights or assuming inappropriate obligations; and

(e) the decision-making process (including reliance on s194 with full disclosure, documentation of rationale, and compliance with CobaltBlu's Conflict Policy) is appropriate given CobaltBlu's current board composition and the impracticability of obtaining a disinterested director approval.

Independent Director Appointment (Future)

The directors note that WaterRoads has committed to appoint an independent director at or within 60 days of Series A close. Once that appointment occurs, WaterRoads-related decisions will benefit from independent oversight, and CobaltBlu (as a WaterRoads shareholder) will have the benefit of that enhanced governance framework.

PART A — SHAREHOLDER RESOLUTIONS

(Passed pursuant to section 249A of the Corporations Act)

The shareholders of CobaltBlu resolve as follows:

Resolution 1 — Approval of Recapitalisation and Participation

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu approve and authorise CobaltBlu's participation in the Recapitalisation of WaterRoads on the terms set out in the Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026, including without limitation:

(a) Surrender and Cancellation of Existing Shares

The surrender for cancellation of CobaltBlu's 1,000 FOU/Founder's shares in WaterRoads for nil consideration, pursuant to the selective reduction of capital approved by WaterRoads shareholders under sections 256B and 256C of the Act.

(b) Acceptance of F Shares

The acceptance of 96,000 F Shares in WaterRoads (being 960,000 F Shares after the 10-for-1 share split contemplated in Resolution 1(d)), issued for nil cash consideration on a share-for-share basis.

(c) Agreed Ownership

The acceptance and acknowledgment that CobaltBlu's post-Recapitalisation shareholding of 96.00% reflects the Agreed Ownership as between CobaltBlu and CBS Group, and represents the correction of Historic Defects in WaterRoads' capital structure as documented in the Recap Deed.

(d) Share Split

The acceptance of the 10-for-1 share split (subdivision) of all WaterRoads shares, such that CobaltBlu's 96,000 F Shares become 960,000 F Shares.

(e) F Share Conversion upon Qualifying Financing

The acceptance and acknowledgment that, upon completion of a Qualifying Financing (as defined in clause 3.1 of the New Constitution), CobaltBlu's F Shares will automatically convert into Common Shares on a 1:1 basis in accordance with clause 4.4 of the New Constitution, without further shareholder action.

(f) Ranking and Rights

The acceptance that the F Shares will rank in accordance with the terms of the New Constitution, including:

Founder Protective Provisions (clause 20) applicable while F Share Majority holds ≥30% on a Fully Diluted Basis;

Founder Director appointment rights (clause 16.2) applicable while F Share Majority holds ≥20% on a Fully Diluted Basis;

Conversion rights and mechanisms (clause 4.4);

Dividend, voting, and other economic and control rights as set out in the New Constitution.

(g) Legal and Tax Consequences

The directors are authorised to obtain such legal, tax, and financial advice as they consider appropriate in connection with the Recapitalisation and to rely on such advice in implementing these resolutions.

Resolution 2 — Approval of New Constitution

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu note, acknowledge, and approve the adoption by WaterRoads of the Amended and Restated Constitution of WaterRoads Pty Ltd — Version 3.1 (the New Constitution), effective 15 January 2026 (or such later date as the WaterRoads special resolution takes effect), including without limitation the following key provisions affecting CobaltBlu's rights as a shareholder:

(a) Two-Class Share Structure

The establishment of a two-class share structure comprising:

F Shares (held by CobaltBlu and any other Founders); and

Common Shares (held by CBS Group and, following Series A, by Series A Investors).

(b) Founder Protective Provisions (Clause 20)

The Founder Protective Provisions in clause 20 of the New Constitution, which require the prior written consent of the F Share Majority (being holders of >50% of F Shares on a Fully Diluted Basis) for the following matters, applicable while the F Share Majority holds ≥30% of all shares on a Fully Diluted Basis:

(i) any amendment to the Constitution that adversely affects the rights of F Share holders;

(ii) any issue of shares ranking senior to or pari passu with F Shares (other than pursuant to a Qualifying Financing or the ESOP);

(iii) any disposal of all or substantially all of the Company's assets;

(iv) any merger, consolidation, or sale of the Company;

(v) any voluntary liquidation or winding up;

(vi) any change in the principal business of the Company; and

(vii) other Reserved Matters as specified in clause 20.2.

(c) Founder Director Appointment Rights (Clause 16.2)

The right of the F Share Majority to appoint one Founder Director to the WaterRoads board, applicable while the F Share Majority holds ≥20% of all shares on a Fully Diluted Basis (clause 16.2).

(d) Automatic F Share Conversion (Clause 4.3)

The automatic conversion of all F Shares into Common Shares on a 1:1 basis upon completion of a Qualifying Financing, being (as defined in clause 3.1) a bona fide equity financing in which WaterRoads issues shares for aggregate gross proceeds of at least A$[●] on arms-length terms approved by the WaterRoads board.

(e) ESOP Pool (Clause 26)

The authorisation of an employee share option plan (ESOP) pool of up to 10% of fully diluted share capital (clause 26), from which grants may be made to employees, directors, and consultants of WaterRoads in accordance with the ESOP Rules and board determinations.

(f) General Provisions

All other provisions of the New Constitution, including provisions relating to:

Dividend and distribution rights

Voting rights (one vote per share)

Transfer restrictions and pre-emptive rights

Board composition and appointment

General meetings and resolutions

Winding up and distribution of surplus assets

Resolution 3 — Approval of CBS Consent and Waiver Deed

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu approve CobaltBlu becoming a party to the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed dated [●] January 2026 (or such other date as the deed is executed), including without limitation:

(a) all consents, acknowledgments, confirmations, and undertakings given by CobaltBlu in that deed;

(b) any obligations assumed by CobaltBlu to comply with the New Constitution and the governance framework established under the Recap Deed; and

(c) the execution and delivery of the deed by an authorised director of CobaltBlu in accordance with section 127 of the Act.

Resolution 4 — Approval of Recapitalisation Deed

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu approve:

(a) CobaltBlu's entry into the Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026 among WaterRoads, CobaltBlu, and CBS Group;

(b) the performance by CobaltBlu of all obligations under that deed, including execution of documents, provision of consents, and compliance with Recap Steps and timelines; and

(c) the exercise by CobaltBlu of all rights under that deed, including enforcement rights if WaterRoads or CBS Group fails to comply with its obligations.

Resolution 5 — Approval of Series A Pursuit and Associated Implications

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu note, acknowledge, and approve WaterRoads' intention to pursue a Series A equity financing following the Recapitalisation, and the following implications for CobaltBlu as a shareholder:

(a) Dilution of Percentage Shareholding

CobaltBlu's percentage shareholding in WaterRoads will be diluted by the issuance of shares to Series A Investors. The quantum and terms of the Series A financing are to be determined by the WaterRoads board acting in accordance with its fiduciary duties, the New Constitution, and WaterRoads' Conflict of Interest Policy (Version 6.0 – Institutional).

The shareholders acknowledge that:

(i) dilution is a necessary and expected consequence of an equity financing;

(ii) the Series A financing is commercially necessary for WaterRoads to execute its business plan and grow the enterprise value of CobaltBlu's investment;

(iii) while CobaltBlu's percentage ownership will decrease, the absolute value of CobaltBlu's shareholding is expected to increase if the Series A financing is successful and WaterRoads executes its business plan; and

(iv) CobaltBlu will retain the protections afforded by the Founder Protective Provisions (while the F Share Majority holds ≥30%) and the Founder Director appointment right (while the F Share Majority holds ≥20%).

(b) Automatic Conversion of F Shares

Upon completion of a Qualifying Financing, CobaltBlu's 960,000 F Shares will automatically convert into 960,000 Common Shares on a 1:1 basis (clause 4.4 of the New Constitution).

Post-conversion, CobaltBlu will hold Common Shares ranking equally with all other Common Shares (including those held by CBS Group and Series A Investors), subject to:

(i) any preferential rights granted to Series A Investors pursuant to a new class of shares (e.g., Preference Shares) issued in the Series A; and

(ii) the rights and obligations set out in the Shareholders Agreement (see paragraph (c) below).

(c) Entry into Shareholders Agreement

Series A Investors will require WaterRoads, CobaltBlu, CBS Group, and potentially the individual shareholders of CobaltBlu (Sarah Margaret Taylor and Jeffrey Alan Dusting) to enter into a Shareholders Agreement governing:

(i) governance and board composition;

(ii) consent rights and reserved matters (likely including investor consent rights that supplement or override the Founder Protective Provisions);

(iii) information and inspection rights;

(iv) transfer restrictions, rights of first refusal, co-sale rights, and drag-along/tag-along provisions;

(v) anti-dilution protections;

(vi) exit mechanisms and liquidation preferences; and

(vii) other customary venture capital or growth equity investment terms.

The shareholders authorise the directors to negotiate and enter into a Shareholders Agreement on behalf of CobaltBlu, subject to:

(A) the terms being consistent with market practice for Series A financings of similar-stage Australian companies;

(B) the directors obtaining legal advice on the terms and implications for CobaltBlu;

(C) the agreement not imposing obligations on CobaltBlu that are materially prejudicial to CobaltBlu's interests as a shareholder or that would prevent CobaltBlu from complying with its own constitution or applicable law; and

(D) any approval requirements under CobaltBlu's constitution being satisfied (including, if applicable, further shareholder approval if the Shareholders Agreement involves a material commitment or disposition by CobaltBlu).

(d) Further Amendments to WaterRoads Constitution

Series A Investors may require further amendments to the WaterRoads Constitution as a condition of their investment, which may include:

(i) creation of a new class of Preference Shares or Series A Shares with preferential dividend, liquidation, or voting rights;

(ii) modifications to board composition requirements to include investor-nominated directors;

(iii) additional Reserved Matters requiring investor consent; and

(iv) changes to transfer restrictions, pre-emptive rights, and exit provisions.

The shareholders authorise the directors to consent (on behalf of CobaltBlu as a WaterRoads shareholder) to such constitutional amendments, subject to:

(A) the amendments being reasonably necessary to facilitate the Series A financing;

(B) the amendments not materially and adversely affecting CobaltBlu's existing rights under the New Constitution (including the Founder Protective Provisions and Founder Director appointment right) without CobaltBlu's express consent; and

(C) the directors obtaining legal advice if the amendments involve complex or unusual terms.

(e) Final Terms Subject to WaterRoads Board and Governance

The shareholders acknowledge that:

(i) the final terms of the Series A financing (including valuation, amount raised, investor identity, Shareholders Agreement terms, and constitutional amendments) are to be determined by the WaterRoads board acting in accordance with its fiduciary duties to WaterRoads and all its shareholders;

(ii) WaterRoads' Conflict of Interest Policy (Version 6.0 – Institutional) establishes procedures for managing the conflicts of Sarah Taylor and Jeff Dusting in their capacity as WaterRoads directors, including:

recusal where appropriate;

reliance on s194 with full disclosure;

Independent Advice for Material Transactions;

appointment of an independent director at or within 60 days of Series A close to provide disinterested oversight;

(iii) CobaltBlu, as a WaterRoads shareholder, will have rights under the New Constitution (including Founder Protective Provisions and consent rights) and the Shareholders Agreement (once executed) to protect its interests; and

(iv) this resolution provides a general authorisation and acknowledgment of the Series A process, and does not constitute approval of specific Series A terms (which may be subject to further CobaltBlu shareholder or director approval depending on their nature and impact on CobaltBlu).

PART B — DIRECTOR RESOLUTIONS

(Passed pursuant to section 248A of the Corporations Act)

The directors of CobaltBlu resolve as follows:

Resolution 6 — Authorisation to Execute Documents

RESOLVED that any one director of CobaltBlu is authorised to execute, on behalf of CobaltBlu, the following documents in accordance with section 127 of the Act (execution by company):

(a) the Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026 (if not already executed);

(b) the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed dated [●] January 2026 (or such other date as the deed is executed);

(b1) the CBS Loan Variation and Waiver Deed between WaterRoads and CBS Group;

(c) any written resolution of WaterRoads shareholders (whether ordinary or special resolution) required to give effect to the Recapitalisation, including:

(i) the special resolution to adopt the New Constitution (section 136(2));

(ii) the special resolution to approve the selective reduction of capital / cancellation of existing shares (sections 256B/256C);

(iii) the ordinary resolution to approve the issue of new shares; and

(iv) the ordinary resolution to approve the 10-for-1 share split;

as documented in the written resolutions titled "WaterRoads Pty Ltd — Written Resolutions of Shareholders (Including Special Resolutions)" dated [●] or such other date as the resolutions are executed;

(d) the Shareholders Agreement to be entered into in connection with the Series A financing (subject to the limitations and conditions in Shareholder Resolution 5(c));

(e) any consent to amendment of the WaterRoads Constitution required to facilitate the Series A financing (subject to the limitations and conditions in Shareholder Resolution 5(d));

(f) any transfer forms, share certificates, or ASIC forms required to record CobaltBlu's updated shareholding in WaterRoads following the Recap Steps;

(g) any notices, consents, waivers, or confirmations reasonably required to implement the Recapitalisation, the Series A financing, or related transactions; and

(h) any other documents reasonably incidental to or in connection with the foregoing, including ancillary agreements, deeds of amendment, and administrative documents.

Manner of execution: Documents may be executed by one director signing alone (if permitted by CobaltBlu's constitution and the relevant document), or by two directors signing together, or by one director and the company secretary signing together, in each case in accordance with section 127 of the Act.

Electronic execution: The directors may execute documents electronically in accordance with applicable law, including the Electronic Transactions Act 1999 (Cth) and any applicable state or territory electronic transactions legislation.

Resolution 7 — Ratification of Prior Actions

RESOLVED that all actions taken by the directors of CobaltBlu prior to the date of these resolutions in connection with the Recapitalisation, the Recap Deed, the CBS Consent Deed, the New Constitution, the Series A financing, and related matters are ratified, confirmed, and approved, including without limitation:

(a) participation in negotiations and discussions with WaterRoads, CBS Group, and their respective advisers;

(b) review and comment on drafts of the Recap Deed, CBS Consent Deed, New Constitution, and related documents;

(c) provision of information, consents, and confirmations to WaterRoads, CBS Group, and their advisers;

(d) engagement with legal, tax, and financial advisers (if any) to obtain advice on the Recapitalisation and its implications for CobaltBlu;

(e) attendance at WaterRoads board meetings and participation in WaterRoads board resolutions (in their capacity as WaterRoads directors) relating to the Recapitalisation; and

(f) any other actions reasonably incidental to the foregoing.

Effect of ratification: This ratification has the effect of confirming that the prior actions were within the authority of the directors and were taken in CobaltBlu's interests, and extinguishes any potential claim that the directors acted without authority or in breach of duty in connection with the ratified actions.

Resolution 8 — Conflict Acknowledgment and s194 Reliance

RESOLVED that the directors:

(a) acknowledge the material personal interests and conflicts of interest disclosed in the "Conflict of Interest Disclosure" section of these resolutions;

(b) confirm that each director has given a Standing Notice under section 192 of the Act, disclosing their ongoing interests in WaterRoads, CBS Group (Jeff), and their spousal relationship, and that those Standing Notices remain in effect and cover all matters addressed in these resolutions;

(c) resolve to vote on, and participate in the consideration of, the resolutions in this document in reliance on section 194 of the Act, which permits directors of a proprietary company to vote on matters in which they have a material personal interest provided the interest has been disclosed under s191 or s192;

(d) record that the commercial rationale for the decisions made in these resolutions is as set out in the "Conflict of Interest Disclosure — Commercial Rationale" section above, and that the directors are satisfied the decisions are in CobaltBlu's interests;

(e) confirm that these resolutions and the decision-making process comply with CobaltBlu's Conflict of Interest — Board Policy (Version 6.0 – Institutional), including:

(i) full disclosure of interests;

(ii) reliance on s194 where no disinterested quorum is available;

(iii) documentation of commercial rationale;

(iv) filing of these resolutions in CobaltBlu's governance records; and

(v) noting of the conflicts in the Register of Interests and Related Party Transaction Register; and

(f) authorise the company secretary (or, if none, either director) to:

(i) file a copy of these resolutions in CobaltBlu's minute book and governance records;

(ii) update the Register of Interests and Related Party Transaction Register maintained under the Conflict of Interest Policy;

(iii) provide a copy of these resolutions to WaterRoads and CBS Group as evidence of CobaltBlu's approval and authorisation; and

(iv) provide a copy to CobaltBlu's legal and tax advisers as required.

EXECUTION

The undersigned, being all of the shareholders and all of the directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd, sign these resolutions in accordance with sections 249A and 248A of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth).

Each signatory signs in their dual capacity as both a shareholder and a director of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd.

COBALTBLU PTY LTD

ACN 103 595 071

WRITTEN RESOLUTION OF THE SOLE SHAREHOLDERS

AND DIRECTORS

Pursuant to section 249A and section 248A of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth)

Date: [INSERT DATE]

CONFIDENTIAL

Version 2.0 — Aligned with Constitution V3.1 and V7 document suite. Clause cross-references corrected (conversion cl 4.3→4.4). This consent is Schedule 4 of the Recapitalisation Deed V7. For comprehensive CobaltBlu governance, see CobaltBlu Shareholder & Director Resolutions V3.0 Institutional.

PREAMBLE

The undersigned, being all of the shareholders and directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd ACN 103 595 071 (CobaltBlu), pass the following resolutions in writing pursuant to section 249A (shareholders) and section 248A (directors) of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth). These resolutions are effective when signed by all shareholders and directors and have the same effect as if passed at a duly convened meeting.

BACKGROUND

A.	CobaltBlu holds 1,000 FOU/Founder’s shares in Water Roads Pty Ltd ACN 686 900 014 (Water Roads or the Company), representing 90.91% of the issued share capital.

B.	The Company proposes to implement a recapitalisation (the Recapitalisation) pursuant to a Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026 (the Recapitalisation Deed) between the Company, CobaltBlu, and CBS Group Pty Ltd (CBS).

C.	The Recapitalisation involves:

(i)	the cancellation of all 1,100 existing shares in the Company (including CobaltBlu’s 1,000 FOU/Founder’s shares);

(ii)	the issue of 100,000 new shares (96,000 F Shares to CobaltBlu and 4,000 Common Shares to CBS);

(iii)	a 10-for-1 share split, increasing total shares to 1,000,000 (960,000 F Shares held by CobaltBlu and 40,000 Common Shares held by CBS); and

(iv)	the adoption of an Amended and Restated Constitution V3.1 for the Company.

D.	Following the Recapitalisation, CobaltBlu will hold 960,000 F Shares representing 96% of the Company’s issued share capital.

E.	The Company intends to pursue a Series A equity financing following the Recapitalisation. Upon completion of a Qualifying Financing (as defined in the Constitution), F Shares will automatically convert into Common Shares.

F.	CobaltBlu is also required to execute, or has been asked to be a party to, the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed in connection with the Recapitalisation.

CONFLICT DISCLOSURE

The directors note the following interests for the purposes of sections 191 and 192 of the Corporations Act:

(a)	Sarah Margaret Taylor is a director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu, a director and Company Secretary of Water Roads, and the spouse of Jeffrey Alan Dusting.

(b)	Jeffrey Alan Dusting is a director and 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu, a director of Water Roads, and a director of CBS Group Pty Ltd.

(c)	Both directors have material personal interests in the Recapitalisation by virtue of:

(i)	their roles as directors and shareholders of CobaltBlu (which holds shares in Water Roads);

(ii)	their roles as directors of Water Roads;

(iii)	Jeffrey Alan Dusting’s additional role as a director of CBS; and

(iv)	their spousal relationship.

(d)	CobaltBlu is a proprietary company with only two directors, both of whom are interested. The directors vote on these resolutions in reliance on section 194 of the Corporations Act.

(e)	Both directors have given standing notices of interest under section 192 of the Corporations Act.

PART A — SHAREHOLDER RESOLUTIONS

(Passed pursuant to section 249A of the Corporations Act)

Resolution 1 — Approval of Recapitalisation

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu approve and authorise CobaltBlu’s participation in the Recapitalisation on the terms set out in the Recapitalisation Deed, including:

(a)	the surrender and cancellation of CobaltBlu’s 1,000 FOU/Founder’s shares in the Company for no consideration;

(b)	the acceptance of 96,000 F Shares in the Company (being 960,000 F Shares after the 10-for-1 share split), issued for nil cash consideration on a share-for-share basis;

(c)	the acceptance that CobaltBlu’s post-Recapitalisation shareholding of 96% reflects the Agreed Ownership as between CobaltBlu and CBS; and

(d)	the acceptance that upon completion of a Qualifying Financing, the F Shares will automatically convert into Common Shares in accordance with clause 4.4 of the Constitution.

Resolution 2 — Approval of New Constitution

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu note and approve the adoption by the Company of the Amended and Restated Constitution V3.1 effective 15 January 2026, including:

(a)	the two-class share structure (F Shares and Common Shares);

(b)	the Founder Protective Provisions in clause 20 of the Constitution (applicable while the F Share Majority holds ≥30% of shares on a Fully Diluted Basis);

(c)	the Founder Director appointment rights in clause 16.2 of the Constitution (applicable while the F Share Majority holds ≥20% of shares on a Fully Diluted Basis);

(d)	the auto-conversion of F Shares into Common Shares upon a Qualifying Financing (clause 4.4); and

(e)	the 10% ESOP pool authorised under clause 26.

Resolution 3 — Approval of CBS Consent and Waiver Deed

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu approve CobaltBlu becoming a party to the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed, including the consents, acknowledgments, and undertakings given by CobaltBlu in that deed.

Resolution 4 — Approval of Recapitalisation Deed

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu approve CobaltBlu’s entry into the Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026, and the performance of all obligations and the exercise of all rights under that deed.

Resolution 5 — Approval of Series A Pursuit

RESOLVED that the shareholders of CobaltBlu note and approve the Company’s intention to pursue a Series A equity financing, which may result in:

(a)	the dilution of CobaltBlu’s percentage shareholding in the Company;

(b)	the automatic conversion of F Shares into Common Shares;

(c)	the entry into a Shareholders Agreement with Series A Investors; and

(d)	further amendments to the Company’s Constitution as required by Series A Investors.

PART B — DIRECTOR RESOLUTIONS

(Passed pursuant to section 248A of the Corporations Act)

Resolution 6 — Authorisation to Execute Documents

RESOLVED that either director of CobaltBlu is authorised to execute, on behalf of CobaltBlu, the following documents in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act:

(a)	the Recapitalisation Deed;

(b)	the CBS Consent and Waiver Deed;

(c)	any written shareholder resolution of the Company required to give effect to the Recapitalisation (including the special resolution to adopt the new Constitution); and

(d)	any other documents reasonably required to implement the Recapitalisation or facilitate the Series A financing.

Resolution 7 — Ratification

RESOLVED that all actions taken by the directors of CobaltBlu prior to the date of these resolutions in connection with the Recapitalisation, the Recapitalisation Deed, and related matters are ratified and confirmed.

Resolution 8 — Conflict Acknowledgment

RESOLVED that the directors acknowledge the conflicts of interest disclosed above, confirm that they have each given standing notices under section 192 of the Corporations Act, and resolve to vote on these resolutions in reliance on section 194 of the Corporations Act (CobaltBlu being a proprietary company with only two directors, both of whom are interested).

EXECUTION

The undersigned, being all of the shareholders and directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd, sign these resolutions in accordance with sections 249A and 248A of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth).

Each signatory signs in their dual capacity as both a shareholder and a director of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd.

END OF RESOLUTIONS



| _______________________________

SARAH MARGARET TAYLOR
Director and 50% Shareholder

Date: _______________________________ |



| _______________________________

JEFFREY ALAN DUSTING
Director and 50% Shareholder

Date: _______________________________ |

CONFIDENTIAL

Version 2.0 — Aligned with Constitution V3.1 and V7 document suite. Clause cross-references corrected (conversion cl 4.3→4.4). This consent is Schedule 4 of the Recapitalisation Deed V7. For comprehensive CobaltBlu governance, see CobaltBlu Shareholder & Director Resolutions V3.0 Institutional.

PREAMBLE

The undersigned, being all of the shareholders and directors of CobaltBlu Pty Ltd ACN 103 595 071 (CobaltBlu), pass the following resolutions in writing pursuant to section 249A (shareholders) and section 248A (directors) of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth). These resolutions are effective when signed by all shareholders and directors and have the same effect as if passed at a duly convened meeting.

BACKGROUND

A.	CobaltBlu holds 1,000 FOU/Founder’s shares in Water Roads Pty Ltd ACN 686 900 014 (Water Roads or the Company), representing 90.91% of the issued share capital.

C.	The Recapitalisation involves:

(i)	the cancellation of all 1,100 existing shares in the Company (including CobaltBlu’s 1,000 FOU/Founder’s shares);

(iii)	a 10-for-1 share split, increasing total shares to 1,000,000 (960,000 F Shares held by CobaltBlu and 40,000 Common Shares held by CBS); and

BOARD PAPER AND RESOLUTIONS

Governance Completion and Series A Cooperation

Note: Jim Ellwood attends as observer to provide external visibility into CobaltBlu governance. Both directors vote under s194. This meeting confirms Series A cooperation commitments.

Agenda Item 1: Welcome and Apologies

The Chair, Sarah Taylor, opened the meeting at 10:00 AM AEDT and welcomed attendees.

Agenda Item 2: Note: Jim Ellwood Attendance as Observer

2.1 Observer Protocol

Jim Ellwood, independent director of CBS Group Pty Ltd, has been invited to attend this meeting as an observer. CBS Group holds 4% of Water Roads Pty Ltd, and CobaltBlu holds 96%.

Agenda Item 3: Confirmation of Previous Minutes

3.1 Background

The minutes of the previous board meeting (CBU-2026-001 held on 15 January 2026) were circulated prior to this meeting.

3.2 Meeting Record — CBU-2026-001

Agenda Item 4: Declarations of Interest

4.1 Standing Notices

Both directors have Standing Notices under section 192 of the Corporations Act in force:

4.2 Section 194 Reliance

CobaltBlu is a proprietary company with only two directors, both of whom have material personal interests in the Water Roads Recapitalisation and Series A. As no disinterested director is available, both directors are entitled to vote pursuant to section 194 of the Corporations Act.

Agenda Item 5: Adoption of CobaltBlu COI Policy V6.0 (Institutional)

5.1 Background

A Conflict of Interest Policy V6.0 (Institutional) has been developed for CobaltBlu, consistent with the policies adopted by Water Roads and CBS Group. This ensures governance alignment across the corporate group.

5.2 Key Features

Agenda Item 6: Executed Documents — Filing

6.1 Documents Executed

The following document was executed by CobaltBlu on 15 January 2026 following the approvals at meeting CBU-2026-001:

Agenda Item 7: CobaltBlu Transmittal Letter

7.1 Background

A CobaltBlu Transmittal Letter has been prepared to confirm to the Water Roads board the completion of CobaltBlu's obligations under the Recapitalisation and CobaltBlu's commitments as majority shareholder ahead of Series A.

7.2 Letter Contents

The CobaltBlu Transmittal Letter confirms:

(a)  CobaltBlu has executed all required Recapitalisation documents

(b)  CobaltBlu's shareholding is 960,000 F Shares (96% of Water Roads)

(c)  CobaltBlu supports the Series A funding round

(d)  CobaltBlu will cooperate with Series A due diligence and investor requests

(e)  CobaltBlu will execute the Shareholders Agreement when presented

7.3 Signatory

The CobaltBlu Transmittal Letter will be signed by Sarah Margaret Taylor as Chair of CobaltBlu.

Agenda Item 8: Confirmation of CobaltBlu Shareholding

8.1 Water Roads Share Register Extract

Following the Recapitalisation and 10:1 share split, CobaltBlu's shareholding in Water Roads is:

8.2 Founder Protective Provisions

The F Shares held by CobaltBlu carry Founder Protective Provisions under clause 20 of the Water Roads Constitution V3.1, including:

(a)  Board composition rights (Founder Director appointment)

(b)  Veto rights over specified matters (constitution amendments, share issues, material transactions)

(c)  Anti-dilution protections

(d)  Exit participation rights (tag-along, drag-along)

(e)  Information rights

Agenda Item 9: Series A Cooperation Commitments

9.1 Background

Water Roads is raising a Series A round of A$15M at A$380M post-money valuation, with Ocean Zero as lead investor (A$10M) and Australian co-investors for the balance (A$5M). Target close is 7 March 2026.

9.2 CobaltBlu Cooperation Requirements

As majority shareholder, CobaltBlu's cooperation is essential for Series A success. Series A investors may request:

(a)  Confirmation of CobaltBlu's shareholding and beneficial ownership

(b)  Copies of executed Recapitalisation documents

(c)  Meeting availability for investor due diligence calls

(d)  Execution of the Shareholders Agreement

(e)  Consent to any Series A-related matters requiring shareholder approval

Agenda Item 10: SHA Approval Process

10.1 Expected Timeline

A Shareholders Agreement (SHA) will be required as part of the Series A closing. The expected timeline is:

10.2 Board Authority

The Board noted that:

(a)  Sarah Taylor has been authorised to execute the SHA on behalf of CobaltBlu (Resolution 3(d))

(b)  This authority is subject to Board review of the final SHA terms

(c)  A further Board meeting will be convened if the SHA contains material terms not previously disclosed

(d)  Circulating resolutions may be used for time-critical approvals if required

Agenda Item 11: Next Meeting

Agenda Item 12: Close

There being no further business, the Chair thanked Jim Ellwood for his attendance as observer and declared the meeting closed at [TIME] AEDT.

Summary of Resolutions

Note: All resolutions passed pursuant to section 194 of the Corporations Act (proprietary company exception). Both directors entitled to vote notwithstanding their material personal interests.

### CBS-BEN-01_Beneficial-Ownership-Declaration_V1.0_TEMPLATE copy.docx

*File: `CBS-BEN-01_Beneficial-Ownership-Declaration_V1.0_TEMPLATE copy.docx`*

CBS-BEN-01_Beneficial-Ownership-Declaration_V1.0_TEMPLATE

BENEFICIAL OWNERSHIP DECLARATION

WATER ROADS HOLDING

1.  Company and holding

CBS Group Pty Ltd (CBS) holds 40,000 Common Shares in Water Roads Pty Ltd ACN 686 900 014 (Water Roads), representing 4% of Water Roads' issued share capital following the Recapitalisation documented in the Recapitalisation Deed dated 15 January 2026.

2.  Beneficial owners

The legal and beneficial ownership of all shares in CBS (and therefore the indirect beneficial ownership of CBS's shares in Water Roads) is held as follows:

3.  Look-through statement

Accordingly, the 40,000 Common Shares in Water Roads held in the name of CBS are beneficially owned as follows:

•  [XX]% by [SHAREHOLDER 1 NAME], indirectly through their shareholding in CBS

•  [XX]% by [SHAREHOLDER 2 NAME], indirectly through their shareholding in CBS

•  [Add/delete rows as needed]

4.  No nominee or trustee arrangements

CBS holds its Water Roads shares on its own behalf and not as trustee, nominee, or bare trustee for any person other than its shareholders named above.

5.  Director independence

Jim Ellwood is an independent director of CBS and [is / is not] a shareholder of CBS. [If shareholder, his interest is disclosed in the table above.]

Jeffrey Alan Dusting is a director of CBS and [is / is not] a shareholder of CBS. [If shareholder, his interest is disclosed in the table above.] Jeff Dusting is also a director of Water Roads and CobaltBlu, and a 50% shareholder of CobaltBlu (which holds 96% of Water Roads). These interests are disclosed in his Standing Notices.

6.  Conflicts and standing notices

Jeffrey Alan Dusting has disclosed his interests in Water Roads and CobaltBlu in standing notices under section 192 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth), tabled at the CBS board in accordance with the CBS Conflict of Interest Policy Version 6.0 (Institutional). Jim Ellwood, as independent director, voted on all CBS board resolutions relating to the Recapitalisation; Jeff Dusting abstained.

7.  Purpose of declaration

This declaration is provided for the purposes of investor due diligence in connection with the Recapitalisation and proposed Series A financing of Water Roads and may be shared with Water Roads' legal and financial advisers and prospective Series A investors.

EXECUTION

Signed for and on behalf of CBS Group Pty Ltd ACN 164 870 080 in accordance with section 127 of the Corporations Act 2001 (Cth):

Date: ___________________ [February] 2026
